### [63] [Semantics-Aware Hierarchical Token Communication: Clustering, Bit Mapping, and Power Allocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27641)
*Jihoon Lee,Seungeun Oh,Jihong Park,Seong-Lyun Kim,Seung-Woo Ko*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 本文提出分层令牌通信（H-TokCom）框架，通过在物理层设计中嵌入语义结构——将语义相似的令牌聚簇并分层分配比特表示（簇级前缀+令牌级后缀），同时为前缀比特分配更多发射功率，从而在低信噪比下减少语义损失。在COCO数据集上，该方案将语义相似度从0.206提升至0.279（增益35.4%）。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有令牌通信（TokCom）采用以AI为中心的设计，依赖大模型进行语义恢复，但其物理层设计（如令牌-比特映射和功率分配）仍是传统方案，未反映令牌级语义信息。这种语义无关的设计在低信噪比下会导致严重的语义损失。

Method: 提出分层令牌通信（H-TokCom）框架，核心思想是将语义相似的令牌聚簇，并分层分配比特表示：每个令牌由簇级前缀和令牌级后缀构成。只要簇比特正确传输，后缀比特错误时接收令牌仍落在同一语义簇内，从而限制语义失真。此外，为前缀比特分配比后缀比特更多的发射功率以进一步增强鲁棒性。

Result: 在COCO数据集上，H-TokCom在考虑的信噪比范围内相较传统TokCom取得了显著的语义相似度增益。在γ=3 dB时，语义相似度从0.206提升至0.279，增益达0.073（35.4%）。

Conclusion: 通过在物理层直接嵌入语义结构，H-TokCom能有效减少低信噪比下的语义损失，显著提升通信系统的语义相似度，为语义通信的物理层设计提供了新思路。

Original Abstract: Despite the rise of token communication (TokCom) as a new paradigm beyond traditional bit communication, existing approaches have primarily adopted artificial intelligence (AI)-centric designs that rely on semantic recovery via large models. Meanwhile, their physical-layer designs, such as token-bit mapping and power allocation, remain conventional and do not reflect token-level semantics. These semantics-agnostic designs can lead to significant semantic loss, particularly at low signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) levels. To address this issue, we propose hierarchical TokCom (H-TokCom), a framework that embeds semantic structure directly into physical-layer design. The key idea is to group semantically similar tokens into clusters and hierarchically assign their bit representations, where each token is represented by a cluster-level prefix and a token-specific suffix. As long as the cluster bits are correctly delivered, errors in the suffix bits typically map the received token to another within the same semantic cluster, resulting in only limited semantic distortion. This robustness is further strengthened by allocating more transmit power to the prefix bits than to the suffix bits. Simulation results show that H-TokCom achieves substantial semantic-similarity gains over conventional TokCom across the considered SNR range, increasing the semantic similarity from $0.206$ to $0.279$ at $γ=3$ dB on COCO, corresponding to a gain of $0.073$ $(35.4\%)$.

中文摘要翻译: 尽管令牌通信（TokCom）作为超越传统比特通信的新范式已经兴起，现有方法主要采用以人工智能（AI）为中心的设计，依赖大模型进行语义恢复。与此同时，它们的物理层设计（如令牌-比特映射和功率分配）仍然是传统的，并未反映令牌级语义信息。这些语义无关的设计会导致显著的语义损失，尤其在低信噪比（SNR）条件下。为解决此问题，我们提出分层令牌通信（H-TokCom），一种将语义结构直接嵌入物理层设计的框架。其核心思想是将语义相似的令牌聚簇，并分层分配它们的比特表示，其中每个令牌由一个簇级前缀和一个令牌级后缀表示。只要簇比特被正确传递，后缀比特的错误通常会将接收令牌映射到同一语义簇内的另一个令牌，从而仅造成有限的语义失真。通过将更多发射功率分配给前缀比特而非后缀比特，这种鲁棒性得到进一步增强。仿真结果表明，在COCO数据集上，H-TokCom在所考虑的信噪比范围内相较传统TokCom取得了显著的语义相似度增益，在γ=3 dB时将语义相似度从0.206提升至0.279，对应增益为0.073（35.4%）。

</details>


### [64] [On the Fractional Fourier Transform for FMCW Radar Interference Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27768)
*Christian Oswald,Josef Kulmer,Franz Pernkopf*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 本文针对FMCW雷达互干扰抑制问题，基于离散分数阶傅里叶变换（DFrFT）提出了一种改进方法，通过稀疏更新信号降低计算复杂度，并实现了多干扰同时抑制，在实际测量数据上验证了有效性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 解决FMCW雷达系统中互干扰抑制问题，降低DFrFT方法的计算复杂度，并使其能够同时应对多个干扰源，从而提升实际应用中的实时性和鲁棒性。

Method: 基于离散分数阶傅里叶变换（DFrFT）的干扰抑制方法；提出包含DFrFT干扰抑制模块的实值接收机雷达信号处理链；通过稀疏更新信号重新形式化DFrFT方法以降低计算复杂度，实现多干扰同时抑制。

Result: 在合成数据集上与参考算法进行了对比验证；实际测量数据的案例研究表明该方法与真实环境兼容。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于DFrFT的互干扰抑制方法通过稀疏更新策略有效降低了计算复杂度且支持多干扰同时抑制，在真实环境中具有可行性。

Original Abstract: In this paper, we extend our method [1] for FMCW radar mutual interference mitigation (IM) based on the discrete fractional Fourier transform (DFrFT). Firstly, we propose a radar signal processing chain including our DFrFT-based IM for real-valued receivers, which we compare to reference algorithms on a synthetic data set. We then reduce computational complexity by reformulating DFrFT-based IM in terms of sparse update signals, which enables mitigation of multiple interferences simultaneously. Finally, we conduct a case study on measurement data and show that our method is compatible with real-world environments.

中文摘要翻译: 本文对我们先前基于离散分数阶傅里叶变换（DFrFT）的FMCW雷达互干扰抑制方法[1]进行了扩展。首先，我们提出了一套面向实值接收机的雷达信号处理链，其中包含了基于DFrFT的干扰抑制模块，并在合成数据集上将其与参考算法进行了比较。随后，我们通过稀疏更新信号重新形式化了基于DFrFT的干扰抑制方法，从而降低了计算复杂度，并实现了对多个干扰的同时抑制。最后，我们基于实际测量数据进行了案例研究，结果表明该方法与真实环境兼容。

### [65] [Sequential Inference for Gaussian Processes: A Signal Processing Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28163)
*Daniel Waxman,Fernando Llorente,Petar M. Djurić*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 本文对高斯过程（GPs）在信号处理中的序贯推理方法进行了综述性介绍，重点阐述了其在流式数据、状态空间建模、时序预测、异常检测、贝叶斯优化等任务中的最新进展，为实际部署序贯GP模型提供了实用工具和路线图。

Method: 本文以教程式综述的方式，从信号处理视角出发，系统介绍高斯过程的序贯推理方法，包括：状态空间建模、序贯回归与预测、时序异常检测、序贯贝叶斯优化、自适应与主动感知、序贯检测与决策等。同时将这些技术桥接到机器学习领域的最新进展。

Result: 本文为综述性质，没有呈现新的实验或分析结果，而是系统梳理和总结了序贯高斯过程模型在多个信号处理任务中的方法论进展，并为实际部署提供了实用工具和路线图。

Original Abstract: The proliferation of capable and efficient machine learning (ML) models marks one of the strongest methodological shifts in signal processing (SP) in its nearly 100-year history. ML models support the development of SP systems that represent complex, nonlinear relationships with high predictive accuracy. Adapting these models often requires sequential inference, which differs both theoretically and methodologically from the usual paradigm of ML, where data are often assumed independent and identically distributed. Gaussian processes (GPs) are a flexible yet principled framework for modeling random functions, and they have become increasingly relevant to SP as statistical and ML methods assume a more prominent role. We provide a self-contained, tutorial-style overview of GPs, with a particular focus on recent methodological advances in sequential, incremental, or streaming inference. We introduce these techniques from a signal-processing perspective while bridging them to recent advances in ML. By organizing these advances from a signal-processing perspective, we intend to equip practitioners with practical tools and a coherent roadmap for deploying sequential GP models in real-world systems.

### [67] [A Two Stage Pipeline for Left Atrial Wall Constrained Scar Segmentation and Localization from LGE-MR Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27101)
*Bipasha Kundu,Cristian Linte*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文提出一个两阶段nnUNet框架，通过解剖结构感知（左心房腔体与壁的符号距离图）和边界不确定性感知损失，解决LGE-MRI中左心房消融瘢痕分割的类别不平衡、壁薄、对比度低等问题，在LAScarQS 2022上达到61.1% Dice和1.711mm ASSD。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: LGE-MRI中左心房消融瘢痕的可靠量化与定位极具挑战：瘢痕体素严重类别不平衡、心房壁结构薄、组织对比度弱，导致预测结果不真实，而准确分割与定位对评估消融完整性及指导治疗至关重要。

Method: 提出两阶段nnUNet框架：第一阶段训练nnUNet分割左心房腔体；第二阶段从预测解剖结构导出患者特定的腔体与壁符号距离图（SDM），作为几何感知输入显式编码体素与心房腔体/壁的符号空间关系，将瘢痕分割转化为解剖条件定位任务。同时提出壁ROI掩膜加权损失结合边界不确定性感知监督策略，将学习限制在心房壁区域并应对类别不平衡。

Result: 在LAScarQS 2022数据集上达到Dice 61.1%、ASSD 1.711mm，有效降低了远离心房壁的假阳性检测。

Conclusion: 该框架通过几何感知监督强制解剖有效性，提高了瘢痕分割与定位的准确性，降低了远离心房壁的假阳性结果，是一种可靠有效的方法。

Original Abstract: Accurate segmentation and localization of left atrial (LA) ablation scars from Late gadolinium enhancement (LGE)-MRI is essential for assessing the lesion completeness and guiding ablation therapy. Incomplete or discontinuous lesions can increase the recurrence rate of the therapy and inaccurate localization can misguide treatment planning. However, reliable quantification and localization of scar in LGE-MRI is challenging. The severely class imbalanced scar voxels, thin structure of the LA wall, and weak tissue contrast often lead to unrealistic scar predictions. In this paper, we propose a two stage nnUNet based framework that takes LA anatomy into account to help with more precise scar localization and segmentation. In the first stage, an nnUNet model is trained to segment the LA cavity. In the second stage, patient specific cavity and wall signed distance maps (SDMs) are derived from the predicted anatomy to use as geometry aware inputs, and explicitly encode each voxel's signed spatial relationship to the atrial cavity and wall. This approach transforms scar segmentation from a solely intensity-based classification into anatomy-conditioned localization task, providing a continuous spatial prior that stabilizes learning for the thin atrial wall and suppresses topologically invalid predictions. To further address boundary ambiguity, we introduce a wall ROI-masked weighted loss combined with boundary uncertainty-aware supervision strategy that restricts learning to the atrial wall, while accounting for severe class imbalance. We evaluated our approach on the LAScarQS 2022 dataset and achieved a Dice of 61.1% and ASSD of 1.711mm. Our reliable and effective framework improves scar segmentation and localization accuracy by enforcing anatomical validity through geometry-aware supervision, and lowering the false positive detections far away from the atrial wall.

中文摘要翻译: 从晚期钆增强磁共振成像（LGE-MRI）中准确分割和定位左心房（LA）消融瘢痕，对于评估消融完整性及指导消融治疗至关重要。不完整或不连续的消融病灶可能增加治疗后的复发率，而定位不准确则可能误导治疗计划。然而，在LGE-MRI中对瘢痕进行可靠的量化与定位极具挑战性。严重类别不平衡的瘢痕体素、左心房壁的薄壁结构以及微弱的组织对比度，常常导致不切实际的瘢痕预测。在本文中，我们提出一个基于nnUNet的两阶段框架，该框架引入左心房解剖结构先验，以辅助更精确的瘢痕定位与分割。第一阶段训练一个nnUNet模型用于分割左心房腔体。第二阶段从预测的解剖结构中导出患者特定的腔体与壁符号距离图（SDM），将其作为几何感知输入，显式编码每个体素与心房腔体和壁的符号空间关系。该方法将瘢痕分割从纯粹基于强度的分类任务转化为解剖条件定位任务，提供一个连续的空间先验，稳定对薄壁心房壁的学习，并抑制拓扑结构无效的预测。为进一步解决边界模糊问题，我们引入一种壁ROI掩膜加权损失，结合边界不确定性感知监督策略，将学习限制在心房壁区域，同时应对严重的类别不平衡。我们在LAScarQS 2022数据集上评估了该方法，实现了61.1%的Dice系数和1.711mm的平均对称表面距离（ASSD）。我们的可靠且有效的框架通过几何感知监督强制执行解剖有效性，提高了瘢痕分割与定位的准确性，并降低了远离心房壁的假阳性检测。

This framework offers a way to incorporate multiple generative priors into OAMP. ### [69] [Monitoring Neural Training with Topology: A Footprint-Predictable Collapse Index](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26984)
*Alexander Kalinowski*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种在线、拓扑感知的监控方法MMHM+CI，通过稀疏编辑和离散Morse匹配高效检测神经表示中的表征坍缩，在LLM微调和时序KGE训练中提供低延迟的早期预警信号。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 表征坍缩（嵌入各向异性、丢失多尺度结构）会在性能指标反应之前就已侵蚀下游性能，现有方法缺乏高效的在线监控手段。

Method: 结合模块化Morse同调维护（MMHM）与复合坍缩指数（CI），在每个epoch进行固定尺度的稀疏编辑，维护离散Morse匹配，实现快速增量更新，无需重建复形。

Result: 在LLM微调和时序知识图谱嵌入训练中，CI作为低延迟预警信号有效，适合训练中的干预。

### [70] [Simple Self-Conditioning Adaptation for Masked Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26985)
*Michael Cardei,Huu Binh Ta,Ferdinando Fioretto*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出自条件掩码扩散模型（SCMDM），通过对掩码扩散模型进行后训练适配，利用模型自身先前的干净状态预测来调节每一步去噪，在不增加推理开销的情况下显著提升生成质量。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 标准掩码扩散模型中，若某位置在反向更新后仍保持掩码状态，模型会丢弃对该位置的干净状态预测，导致仍被掩码的位置只能从掩码token反复推断，限制了跨步精化能力。

Method: SCMDM是一种后训练适配方法，将每一步去噪过程条件化在模型自身上一轮生成的干净状态预测上。该方法只需最小限度的架构改动，不引入循环潜在状态路径，不依赖辅助参考模型，且在采样过程中不增加额外去噪器评估次数。

Result: 在多个领域取得一致改进：OWT训练模型生成困惑度降低近50%（42.89降至23.72），在离散图像合成、小分子生成和基因组分布建模等方面均有显著提升。

Conclusion: 部分自条件化（如常见的50%丢弃策略）在后训练场景中是次优的；一旦模型自生成的干净状态估计变得有信息量，专门进行精化比混合条件与非条件目标更优。

Original Abstract: Masked diffusion models (MDMs) generate discrete sequences by iterative denoising under an absorbing masking process. In standard masked diffusion, if a token remains masked after a reverse update, the model discards its clean-state prediction for that position. Thus, still-masked positions must be repeatedly inferred from the mask token alone. This design choice limits cross-step refinement. To address this limitation, this paper proposes a simple, yet effective, post-training adaptation for MDMs that conditions each denoising step on the model's own previous clean-state predictions. The resulting method, called Self-Conditioned Masked Diffusion Models (SCMDM), requires minimal architectural change, does not introduce a recurrent latent-state pathway, does not rely on an auxiliary reference model, and adds no extra denoiser evaluations during sampling. This is an important departure from partial self-conditioning approaches which requires expensive model training from scratch. In particular, the paper shows that partial self-conditioning, including the commonly used 50% dropout strategy for training self-conditioned models from scratch, is suboptimal in the post-training regime. Instead, once the model's self-generated clean-state estimates become informative, the specialization to refinement is preferable to mixing conditional and unconditional objectives. SCMDM is evaluated across multiple domains, demonstrating consistent improvement over vanilla MDM baselines, achieving nearly a 50% reduction in generative perplexity on OWT-trained models (42.89 to 23.72), alongside strong improvements in discretized image synthesis quality, small molecular generation, and enhanced fidelity in genomic distribution modeling.

中文摘要翻译: 掩码扩散模型（MDMs）通过在吸收性掩码过程下的迭代去噪来生成离散序列。在标准的掩码扩散中，如果一个token在反向更新后仍保持掩码状态，模型会丢弃该位置的干净状态预测。因此，仍被掩码的位置必须仅从掩码token反复推断。这种设计选择限制了跨步精化能力。为了解决这一局限性，本文提出一种简单而有效的掩码扩散模型后训练适配方法，将每一步去噪条件化在模型自身先前生成的干净状态预测上。由此产生的SCMDM方法只需极小的架构改动，不引入循环潜在状态路径，不依赖辅助参考模型，且在采样过程中不增加额外的去噪器评估次数。这与需要从头进行昂贵模型训练的局部自条件化方法有本质区别。特别地，本文表明，局部自条件化（包括从头训练自条件模型时常用的50%丢弃策略）在后训练场景中是次优的。相反，一旦模型自生成的干净状态估计变得有信息量，专门进行精化比混合条件与非条件目标更优。SCMDM在多个领域进行了评估，在OWT训练模型上生成困惑度降低近50%（从42.89降至23.72），同时在离散图像合成质量、小分子生成以及基因组分布建模的保真度方面均有显著提升。

</details>


### [71] [People-Centred Medical Image Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26991)
*Zheng Zhang,Milad Masroor,Cuong Nguyen,Tahir Hassan,Yuanhong Chen,David Rosewarne,Kevin Wells,Thanh-Toan Do,Gustavo Carneiro*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出人本医疗影像分析框架PecMan，通过动态门控机制在临床工作负载约束下联合优化公平性、诊断准确率和工作流效率，并引入FairHAI基准评估三者间的权衡。实验表明PecMan持续优于现有方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有数据中心的医学AI系统虽诊断精度高，但因忽视跨人群公平性优化和临床工作流整合而未被广泛采纳；先前的工作流集成方法（如L2D、L2C）与AI公平性研究相互孤立，未考虑临床环境中医生可用性受限等实际约束。

Method: 提出PecMan框架，采用动态门控机制，在医生工作负载约束下将病例智能分配给AI处理、医生处理或两者共同处理，联合优化公平性、诊断准确率和工作流有效性。

Original Abstract: Recent advances in data-centric medical AI have produced highly accurate diagnostic systems, but the emphasis on data curation and performance metrics has not translated into widespread clinical adoption. We conjecture that this limited uptake stems from insufficient attention dedicated to the optimisation of fair performance across diverse patient populations and to workflow integration: performance biases can create regulatory barriers, and poorly integrated automation can disrupt clinical routines, degrade the quality of human-AI collaboration, and reduce clinicians' willingness to adopt AI tools. Prior work on workflow integration (e.g., Learning to Defer (L2D) and Learning to Complement (L2C)) and AI fairness has typically examined these challenges in isolation, overlooking their natural interdependence and the practical constraints of clinical environments, such as restricted clinician availability. We propose People-Centred Medical Image Analysis (PecMan), a human-AI framework that jointly optimises fairness, diagnostic accuracy, and workflow effectiveness through a dynamic gating mechanism that assigns cases to AI, clinicians, or both under clinician workload constraints. We also introduce the Fairness and Human-Centred AI (FairHAI) benchmark for evaluating trade-offs between accuracy, fairness, and clinician workload. Experiments using this benchmark show that PecMan consistently outperforms existing methods, paving the way for more trustworthy and clinically viable AI systems. Code will be available upon paper acceptance.

中文摘要翻译: 近期数据中心的医学AI取得了高度准确的诊断系统，但对数据整理和性能指标的强调并未转化为广泛的临床采纳。我们推测，这种有限的采纳源于对优化跨不同患者群体的公平性能以及工作流整合方面的关注不足：性能偏差可能造成监管障碍，集成不当的自动化可能干扰临床常规、降低人机协作质量并减少临床医生采用AI工具的意愿。先前关于工作流集成（如学习推迟L2D和学习互补L2C）及AI公平性的研究通常孤立地审视这些挑战，忽视了它们自然的相互依赖性以及临床环境的实际约束（如医生可用性受限）。我们提出人本医疗影像分析（PecMan），一种人机协作框架，通过动态门控机制在医生工作负载约束下将病例分配给AI、临床医生或两者共同处理，从而联合优化公平性、诊断准确率和工作流有效性。我们还引入了公平性与人本AI（FairHAI）基准，用于评估准确性、公平性和医生工作负载之间的权衡。利用该基准的实验表明，PecMan持续优于现有方法，为更可信、临床可行的AI系统铺平了道路。代码将在论文接收后公开。

### [72] [Automatic Causal Fairness Analysis with LLM-Generated Reporting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27011)
*Alessia Berarducci,Eric Rossetto,Alessandro Antonucci,Marco Zaffalon*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出FairMind原型工具，利用因果反事实推理和标准公平模型实现数据集层面的自动化公平性分析，并结合LLM生成报告，弥补了现有AutoML框架忽视公平性问题的不足。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有大多数AutoML框架在自动化机器学习流程时，未能考虑训练数据和预测结果中可能存在的公平性缺失问题，亟需一种能够在数据集层面自动化进行公平性分析的工具。

Method: 基于Plečko和Bareinboim提出的标准公平模型，利用因果效应的反事实查询（涉及目标变量、可能的混杂因子和中介变量，以及受保护特征的不同取值）进行公平性评估；在数据预处理后实现效应的闭式求解；采用零样本LLM生成公平性检测报告。

Result: 通过示例展示了该方法相比直接使用LLM进行分析的优势；同时提出了对有序保护变量和连续目标变量的扩展以及新的分解结果。

Conclusion: FairMind作为一种软件原型，能够有效地在数据集层面自动化公平性分析，为AutoML框架融入公平性考量提供了可行的技术路径。

Original Abstract: AutoML, intended as the process of automating the application of machine learning to real-world problems, is a key step for AI popularisation. Most AutoML frameworks are not accounting for the potential lack of fairness in the training data and in the corresponding predictions. We introduce \textsc{FairMind}, a software prototype aiming to automatise fairness analysis at the dataset level. We achieve that by resorting to the assumptions of the \emph{standard fairness model}, recently proposed by Plečko and Bareinboim. This allows for a sound fairness evaluation in terms of causal effects, based on \emph{counterfactual} queries involving the target, possibly confounders and mediators, and the different values of an input feature we regard as \emph{protected}. After the necessary data preprocessing, the tool implements a closed-form computation of the effects. LLMs are consequently exploited to generate accurate reports on the fairness levels detected in the training dataset. We achieve that in a zero-shot setup and show by examples the expected advantages with respect to a direct analysis performed by the LLM. To favour applications, extensions to ordinal protected variable and continuous targets and novel decomposition results are also discussed.

中文摘要翻译: 自动机器学习（AutoML），即自动化地将机器学习应用于现实问题的过程，是推动人工智能普及的关键步骤。然而，大多数AutoML框架并未考虑训练数据及其对应预测中可能存在的公平性缺失问题。本文介绍\textsc{FairMind}，一个旨在实现数据集层面公平性分析自动化的软件原型。我们通过借助Plečko和Bareinboim最近提出的\textit{标准公平模型}的假设来实现这一目标。该方法基于涉及目标变量、可能的混杂因子和中介变量，以及我们视为\textit{受保护}的输入特征的不同取值的\textit{反事实}查询，以因果效应的方式实现了可靠的公平性评估。在必要的数据预处理之后，该工具实现了效应的闭式求解。进而利用大语言模型（LLM）在零样本设置下生成关于训练数据集中检测到的公平性水平的准确报告。通过示例展示了该方法相对于直接由LLM进行分析的预期优势。此外，还讨论了对有序保护变量和连续目标变量的扩展，以及新的分解结果，以促进实际应用。

Method: 使用DeepSeek-R1、OpenBioLLM-Llama3和Qwen 3.5三种大语言模型，在指定ICD-10编码条件下生成合成精神健康评估报告；并引入综合评估框架，从语义保真度、词汇多样性和隐私/抄袭三个维度对生成的诊断文本进行评价。

Original Abstract: The scarcity of high-quality annotated medical data, particularly in mental health, poses a significant bottleneck for training robust machine learning models. ### [74] [PROMISE-AD: Progression-aware Multi-horizon Survival Estimation for Alzheimer's Disease Progression and Dynamic Tracking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28055)
*Qing Lyu,Jeremy Hudson,Mohammad Kawas,Yuming Jiang,Chenyu You,Christopher T Whitlow*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出PROMISE-AD，一种基于生存分析的安全无泄漏框架，用于预测认知正常（CN）向轻度认知障碍（MCI）以及MCI向阿尔茨海默病（AD）痴呆的转化。该方法利用时间Transformer融合全局、注意力池化和最近访问表征，结合离散时间混合风险与多项正则化损失，在ADNI/TADPOLE数据上实现了领先的预测性能，尤其在MCI-to-AD转化中C-index达0.894，5年AUROC达0.997。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有的阿尔茨海默病进展预测模型存在数据泄露、忽略删失数据、无法处理不规则访视、缺乏校准的多时间点风险估计等问题，亟需一种既能利用纵向临床数据又不会引入诊断泄露的生存分析框架。

Method: 将访视前数据转换为包含标准化测量、缺失掩码、纵向变化、时间归一化斜率、访视时间及非诊断类别属性的令牌序列；采用时间Transformer融合全局表征、注意力池化表征和最新访视表征，估计进展分数和潜在离散时间混合风险；训练结合生存似然、时间点特定焦点风险损失、进展排序、风险平滑和混合平衡正则化，再通过验证集等渗校准获得1/2/3/5年风险。

Result: CN-to-MCI转化：IBS 0.085±0.012，C-index 0.808±0.015，平均时变AUC 0.840±0.081，IBS为所有方法中最低；MCI-to-AD转化：C-index 0.894±0.018（最高），5年AUROC 0.997±0.003，AUPRC 0.999±0.001（接近天花板）。消融实验表明纵向变化特征、融合时间表征、混合风险、认知与功能测量、APOE4状态和近期转化前访视均贡献显著。

Conclusion: 进展感知的生存建模能够为AD多时间点转化风险提供可解释且高精度的估计，PROMISE-AD框架在避免数据泄露的同时实现了卓越的预测性能。

Original Abstract: Individualized Alzheimer's disease (AD) progression prediction requires models that use irregular visits, account for censoring, avoid diagnostic leakage, and provide calibrated horizon risks. We propose PROgression-aware MultI-horizon Survival Estimation for Alzheimer's Disease (PROMISE-AD), a leakage-safe survival framework for predicting conversion from cognitively normal (CN) to mild cognitive impairment (MCI) and from MCI to AD dementia using ADNI/TADPOLE tabular histories. PROMISE-AD converts pre-index visits into tokens with standardized measurements, missingness masks, longitudinal changes, time-normalized slopes, visit timing, and non-diagnostic categorical attributes. A temporal Transformer fuses global, attention-pooled, and latest-visit representations to estimate a progression score and latent discrete-time mixture hazards. Training combines survival likelihood, horizon-specific focal risk loss, progression ranking, hazard smoothness, and mixture-balance regularization, followed by validation-set isotonic calibration for 1-, 2-, 3-, and 5-year risks. In held-out testing across three seeds, PROMISE-AD achieved an integrated Brier score (IBS) of 0.085 $\pm$ 0.012, C-index of 0.808 $\pm$ 0.015, and mean time-dependent AUC of 0.840 $\pm$ 0.081 for CN-to-MCI conversion, yielding the lowest IBS among compared methods. For MCI-to-AD conversion, PROMISE-AD achieved the highest C-index (0.894 $\pm$ 0.018) and near-ceiling 5-year discrimination (AUROC 0.997 $\pm$ 0.003; AUPRC 0.999 $\pm$ 0.001), although some baselines had lower IBS. Ablations and interpretability supported longitudinal change features, fused temporal representations, mixture hazards, cognitive and functional measures, APOE4 status, and recent conversion-proximal visits. These findings suggest that progression-aware survival modeling can provide interpretable multi-horizon AD conversion risk estimates.

中文摘要翻译: 个体化的阿尔茨海默病（AD）进展预测需要能够处理不规则访视、考虑删失、避免诊断泄露并提供校准后多时间点风险的模型。我们提出用于阿尔茨海默病的进展感知多时间点生存估计框架（PROMISE-AD），这是一种无泄露的生存框架，利用ADNI/TADPOLE的表格历史数据预测从认知正常（CN）向轻度认知障碍（MCI）以及从MCI向AD痴呆的转化。PROMISE-AD将访视前数据转换为令牌，包含标准化测量、缺失掩码、纵向变化、时间归一化斜率、访视时间以及非诊断类别属性。一个时间Transformer融合全局表征、注意力池化表征和最新访视表征，以估计进展分数和潜在离散时间混合风险。训练结合生存似然、时间点特定焦点风险损失、进展排序、风险平滑和混合平衡正则化，随后通过验证集等渗校准获得1年、2年、3年和5年风险。在三种随机种子下的保留测试中，PROMISE-AD在CN-to-MCI转化上取得了积分布里尔分数（IBS）0.085±0.012、C-index 0.808±0.015和平均时变AUC 0.840±0.081，在对比方法中IBS最低。对于MCI-to-AD转化，PROMISE-AD取得了最高的C-index（0.894±0.018）和接近天花板水平的5年区分性能（AUROC 0.997±0.003；AUPRC 0.999±0.001），尽管某些基线方法的IBS更低。消融研究和可解释性分析支持了纵向变化特征、融合时间表征、混合风险、认知与功能测量、APOE4状态以及近期转化前访视的重要性。这些发现表明，进展感知的生存建模能够为AD多时间点转化提供可解释的风险估计。

</details>


### [75] [Dynamic Adversarial Fine-Tuning Reorganizes Refusal Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27019)
*Wenhao Lan,Shan Li,Junbin Yang,Haihua Shen,Yijun Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过测量驱动的机制研究，分析了7B参数语言模型在监督微调（SFT）和R2D2动态对抗微调下拒绝行为随训练的变化。R2D2早期将拒绝成功率压至0.000，随后部分回升至0.250；几何分析表明拒绝载体从后期层迁移到早期层，支持重组假说而非单纯漂移假说。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 尽管已有研究描述了语言模型的拒绝方向和对越狱攻击的鲁棒性，但动态对抗微调如何改变拒绝载体的训练过程机制尚不清楚。本文旨在揭示这一机制，理解安全性对齐中拒绝行为与过度拒绝之间的权衡。

Method: 采用测量驱动的机制研究方法，在7B骨干模型上进行SFT和R2D2风格的动态对抗微调。实验协议包括：固定源的HarmBench、StrongREJECT和XSTest评估，配合五锚点拒绝几何分析套件和因果干预分析。

Result: R2D2在第50和100步时将固定源HarmBench ASR（攻击成功率）压至0.000，随后在第250步部分回升至0.035，第500步升至0.250；SFT鲁棒性较差，ASR在0.505-0.588之间。XSTest上R2D2的any-refusal早期为1.000，后降至0.664和0.228。几何上，R2D2在第100步前保持后期层可接受载体，之后迁移至早期层载体，有效秩保持在1.23-1.27附近。因果干预表明低维但效用耦合的控制。

Conclusion: 研究结果支持拒绝载体的重组假说（reorganization account）而非单纯的漂移假说（drift-only account），但证据限于单一骨干模型和固定源攻击。

Original Abstract: Safety-aligned language models must refuse harmful requests without collapsing into broad over-refusal, but the training-time mechanisms behind this tradeoff remain unclear. Prior work characterizes refusal directions and jailbreak robustness, yet does not explain how dynamic adversarial fine-tuning changes refusal carriers across training. We present a measurement-driven mechanism study, not a new defense, on one 7B backbone under supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and R2D2-style dynamic adversarial fine-tuning. Our protocol aligns fixed-source HarmBench, StrongREJECT, and XSTest with a five-anchor refusal-geometry suite and causal interventions. R2D2 drives fixed-source HarmBench ASR to 0.000 at steps 50 and 100, then partially reopens to 0.035 at step 250 and 0.250 at step 500; SFT remains less robust, with ASR between 0.505 and 0.588 at the same anchors. On XSTest, R2D2 any-refusal is 1.000 early, then falls to 0.664 and 0.228. Geometrically, R2D2 preserves a late-layer admissible carrier through step 100 before relocating to an early-layer carrier, while effective rank remains near 1.23--1.27. Causal interventions indicate low-dimensional but utility-coupled control. These results support a reorganization account rather than a drift-only account, with evidence limited to one backbone and fixed-source attacks.

中文摘要翻译: 安全对齐的语言模型必须拒绝有害请求，同时避免崩溃为广泛的过度拒绝，但这一权衡背后的训练时机制仍不清楚。先前的研究描述了拒绝方向和越狱鲁棒性，但并未解释动态对抗微调如何改变训练过程中拒绝载体的变化。我们提出一项测量驱动的机制研究（而非新的防御方法），在一个7B骨干模型上进行监督微调（SFT）和R2D2风格的动态对抗微调。我们的实验协议将固定源的HarmBench、StrongREJECT和XSTest与五锚点拒绝几何分析套件及因果干预对齐。R2D2在第50和100步时将固定源HarmBench的攻击成功率（ASR）压至0.000，随后在第250步部分回升至0.035，第500步升至0.250；相比之下，SFT鲁棒性较差，相同锚点下ASR在0.505至0.588之间。在XSTest上，R2D2的any-refusal早期为1.000，随后降至0.664和0.228。几何分析表明，R2D2在第100步前保留了后期层的可接受载体，之后迁移至早期层载体，而有效秩保持在1.23-1.27附近。因果干预表明存在低维但效用耦合的控制。这些结果支持重组假说而非单纯漂移假说，但证据仅限于单一骨干模型和固定源攻击。

</details>


### [76] [Cross-Subject Generalization for EEG Decoding: A Survey of Deep Learning Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27033)

Original Abstract: Deep learning for cross-subject EEG decoding is hindered by high inter-subject variability, which introduces a severe domain shift between training and unseen test subjects. This survey presents a comprehensive review of deep learning methodologies specifically engineered to address this cross-subject generalization challenge. To ground this analysis, we formalize the cross-subject setting as a multi-source domain problem and delineate the rigorous, subject-independent evaluation protocols required for valid assessment. ### [77] [Statistical Channel Fingerprint Construction for Massive MIMO: A Unified Tensor Learning Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27574)
*Zhenzhou Jin,Li You,Xiang-Gen Xia,Xiqi Gao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于张量学习的统一框架LPWTNet，用于从部分观测数据中恢复大规模MIMO通信系统中的统计信道指纹（sCF），通过拉普拉斯金字塔分解、共享掩码学习和小核卷积（基于小波变换）实现高效且精确的sCF重建。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有信道指纹（CF）方法主要依赖瞬时CSI，在数据采集成本、隐私和安全性方面存在实际约束。本文旨在探索一种新型统计信道指纹（sCF），通过存储统计CSI（sCSI）来缓解上述问题，并解决其在不完整/有损条件下的重建难题。

Method: 1) 揭示了sCSI（信道空间协方差矩阵CSCM）与信道功率角谱（CPAS）之间的关系，构建了sCF的统一张量表示；2) 利用CSCM特征值分解及其与PAS的关联进行降维；3) 提出LPWTNet：包含闭环拉普拉斯金字塔（LP）分解与重构框架替代传统编解码器，结合共享掩码学习策略自适应优化高频sCF分量，以及基于小波变换（WT）的小核卷积机制以扩大感受野并提升特征提取效率。

Result: 大量实验表明，所提方法在各种sCF构建场景下，相比现有基线方法均取得了具有竞争力的重建精度和计算效率。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于张量的统一学习架构LPWTNet，通过创新的LP分解重构、共享掩码学习和小波变换卷积机制，能够高效且准确地从不完整观测中重建统计信道指纹，兼顾了性能与计算效率。

Original Abstract: Channel fingerprint (CF) is considered a key enabler for facilitating the acquisition of channel state information (CSI) in massive multiple-input multiple-output (MIMO) communication systems. In this work, we investigate a novel type of CF that stores statistical CSI (sCSI) at each potential location, referred to as statistical CF (sCF). Specifically, we reveal the relationship between sCSI, namely the channel spatial covariance matrix (CSCM), and the channel power angular spectrum (CPAS). Building on this foundation, we construct a unified tensor representation of the sCF and further reduce its dimension by exploiting the eigenvalue decomposition of the CSCM and its correlation with the PAS. Considering the practical constraints imposed by measurement cost, privacy, and security, we focus on three representative scenarios and uniformly formulate them as tensor restoration tasks. To this end, we propose a unified tensor-based learning architecture, termed LPWTNet. The architecture incorporates a closed-form Laplacian pyramid (LP) decomposition and reconstruction framework that replaces the traditional encoder-decoder structure, enabling efficient inference while capturing multi-scale frequency subband characteristics of the sCF. Additionally, a shared mask learning strategy is introduced to adaptively refine high-frequency sCF components through level-wise adjustments. To achieve a larger receptive field without over-parameterization, we further propose a small-kernel convolution mechanism based on the wavelet transform (WT), which decouples convolution across different frequency components of the sCF and enhances feature extraction efficiency. Extensive experiments show that the proposed approach delivers competitive reconstruction accuracy and computational efficiency across various sCF construction scenarios when compared with state-of-the-art baselines.

中文摘要翻译: 信道指纹（CF）被认为是促进大规模多输入多输出（MIMO）通信系统中信道状态信息（CSI）获取的关键使能技术。本文研究了一种新型的CF，它在每个潜在位置存储统计CSI（sCSI），称为统计CF（sCF）。具体来说，我们揭示了sCSI（即信道空间协方差矩阵CSCM）与信道功率角谱（CPAS）之间的关系。在此基础上，构建了sCF的统一张量表示，并利用CSCM的特征值分解及其与PAS的相关性进一步降维。考虑到测量成本、隐私和安全性带来的实际约束，我们聚焦于三个代表性场景，并将其统一建模为张量恢复任务。为此，提出了一种统一的基于张量的学习架构，即LPWTNet。该架构包含一个闭环拉普拉斯金字塔（LP）分解与重构框架，替代传统的编码器-解码器结构，在捕获sCF多尺度频率子带特性的同时实现高效推理。此外，引入了一种共享掩码学习策略，通过逐级调整自适应地优化高频sCF分量。为了在不导致过参数化的前提下获得更大的感受野，我们进一步提出了一种基于小波变换（WT）的小核卷积机制，该机制将sCF不同频率分量的卷积解耦，提升了特征提取效率。大量实验表明，与最先进的基线方法相比，所提方法在各种sCF构建场景下均能提供具有竞争力的重建精度和计算效率。

### [78] [Learning Rate Transfer in Normalized Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27077)
*Boris Shigida,Boris Hanin,Andrey Gromov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对nGPT在学习率跨模型维度与token步数时迁移失败的问题，提出新的参数化方法νGPT，通过结合对齐指数重新设计μP方法，实现了学习率在宽度、深度和token步数上的有效迁移。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: nGPT虽然在训练加速方面表现优异，但其学习率无法在模型维度（宽度、深度）和token步数上进行迁移，这限制了超参数的可扩展性和实际应用效率。

Method: 将数值实验与对齐指数（alignment exponents）原理相结合，重新审视并修改μP超参数迁移方法，提出新的nGPT参数化方案νGPT。

Result: 通过广泛的经验验证，νGPT在宽度、深度和token步数三个维度上均实现了学习率的有效迁移。

Original Abstract: The Normalized Transformer, or nGPT (arXiv:2410.01131) achieves impressive training speedups and does not require weight decay or learning rate warmup. However, despite having hyperparameters that explicitly scale with model size, we observe that nGPT does not exhibit learning rate transfer across model dimension and token horizon. To rectify this, we combine numerical experiments with a principled use of alignment exponents (arXiv:2407.05872) to revisit and modify the $μ$P approach to hyperparameter transfer (arXiv:2011.14522). The result is a novel nGPT parameterization we call $ν$GPT. Through extensive empirical validation, we find $ν$GPT exhibits learning rate transfer across width, depth, and token horizon.

中文摘要翻译: 归一化Transformer（即nGPT，arXiv:2410.01131）在训练加速方面取得了显著成效，且无需权重衰减或学习率预热。然而，尽管其超参数明确随模型规模缩放，我们观察到nGPT在学习率上无法在模型维度和token步数之间进行迁移。为解决此问题，我们将数值实验与对齐指数（arXiv:2407.05872）的原理性使用相结合，重新审视并修改了μP超参数迁移方法（arXiv:2011.14522）。由此得到一种新的nGPT参数化方案，称为νGPT。通过广泛的经验验证，我们发现νGPT在学习率上能够在宽度、深度和token步数之间实现迁移。

### [79] [Co-Evolving Policy Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27083)
*Naibin Gu,Chenxu Yang,Qingyi Si,Chuanyu Qin,Dingyu Yao,Peng Fu,Zheng Lin,Weiping Wang,Nan Duan,Jiaqi Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了协同进化策略蒸馏（CoPD），一种融合RLVR与OPD的统一后训练框架，通过并行训练专家并在专家RLVR训练过程中引入双向OPD，实现多种能力（文本、图像、视频推理）的单模型整合，显著优于混合RLVR和MOPD等基线方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有两种主流后训练范式（混合RLVR和先训练专家再OPD）在将多种专家能力整合到单一模型时各有缺陷：混合RLVR存在能力间发散代价，而流水线式先训练专家再OPD则因师生行为模式差异大而无法充分吸收教师能力。因此，需要一种能同时避免上述问题的新方法。

Method: 提出协同进化策略蒸馏（CoPD），核心思想是：并行训练多个专家，在每位专家进行RLVR训练的过程中（而非训练完成后）同步引入OPD，专家之间互为教师（即双向OPD），从而实现协同进化。这种方法使得专家间的行为模式更加一致，同时保持足够的互补知识。

Result: 实验证明CoPD实现了文本、图像和视频推理能力的全合一整合，显著优于混合RLVR和MOPD等强基线方法，甚至超越领域专用专家模型。

Conclusion: CoPD提供了一种全新的模型并行训练范式，有望启发新的训练扩展范式。

Original Abstract: RLVR and OPD have become standard paradigms for post-training. We provide a unified analysis of these two paradigms in consolidating multiple expert capabilities into a single model, identifying capability loss in different ways: mixed RLVR suffers from inter-capability divergence cost, while the pipeline of first training experts and then performing OPD, though avoiding divergence, fails to fully absorb teacher capabilities due to large behavioral pattern gaps between teacher and student. We propose Co-Evolving Policy Distillation (CoPD), which encourages parallel training of experts and introduces OPD during each expert's ongoing RLVR training rather than after complete expert training, with experts serving as mutual teachers (making OPD bidirectional) to co-evolve. This enables more consistent behavioral patterns among experts while maintaining sufficient complementary knowledge throughout. Experiments validate that CoPD achieves all-in-one integration of text, image, and video reasoning capabilities, significantly outperforming strong baselines such as mixed RLVR and MOPD, and even surpassing domain-specific experts. The model parallel training pattern offered by CoPD may inspire a novel training scaling paradigm.

中文摘要翻译: RLVR（强化学习与值函数推理）和OPD（在线策略蒸馏）已成为后训练的标准范式。我们对这两种范式中将多种专家能力整合到单一模型的问题进行了统一分析，识别出不同方式的能力损失：混合RLVR遭受能力间发散代价，而先训练专家再执行OPD的流水线方式虽然避免了发散，但由于师生之间巨大的行为模式差异，未能完全吸收教师能力。我们提出了协同进化策略蒸馏（CoPD），该方法鼓励专家并行训练，并在每位专家进行中的RLVR训练过程中（而非专家完全训练完成后）引入OPD，专家之间互为教师（使OPD变为双向），从而实现协同进化。这使得专家间的行为模式更加一致，同时在整个过程中保持充分的互补知识。实验验证了CoPD实现了文本、图像和视频推理能力的全合一整合，显著优于混合RLVR和MOPD等强基线方法，甚至超越了领域专用专家。CoPD提供的模型并行训练模式有望启发一种新颖的训练扩展范式。

### [80] [AutoSP: Unlocking Long-Context LLM Training Via Compiler-Based Sequence Parallelism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27089)
*Ahan Gupta,Zhihao Wang,Neel Dani,Masahiro Tanaka,Olatunji Ruwase,Minjia Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AutoSP 是首个自动优化长上下文 LLM 训练的解决方案，通过自动序列并行和长上下文感知的激活检查点技术，在不显著影响吞吐量的前提下，将训练上下文长度提升至 2.7 倍（NVIDIA）和 2.5 倍（AMD）。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有 LLM 训练库（如 ZeRO-3/FSDP、张量并行、流水线并行）主要针对大参数模型优化，缺乏对长上下文训练的高层抽象支持。用户需要手动组合序列并行等复杂优化技术，这要求深厚的专业知识且降低开发效率。

Method: AutoSP 通过编译模型自动应用以下优化：(1) 自动序列并行——自动将长序列切分到多个设备上并行处理；(2) 长上下文感知的激活检查点——根据上下文长度智能选择关键激活值存储策略，减少显存占用。

Result: 在 NVIDIA 和 AMD 硬件上，AutoSP 相比手工编写的最优基线，训练上下文长度分别提升 2.7 倍和 2.5 倍，且运行时性能开销可忽略不计。

Conclusion: AutoSP 是首个自动化长上下文 LLM 训练优化方案，在多种硬件平台上均能显著提升训练上下文长度，且无需用户具备深厚的分布式训练优化专业知识。

Original Abstract: Large-language-models (LLMs) demonstrate enormous utility in long-context tasks which require processing prompts that consist of tens to hundreds of thousands of tokens. However, existing LLM training libraries do not provide easy to use abstractions to optimize for long-context training, instead focusing on optimizations for models with large parameter counts through ZeRO-3/FSDP, Tensor and Pipeline parallelism. This forces users to rewrite LLM training libraries to incorporate compositions of various complex long-context optimizations, such as sequence-parallelism, to training pipelines; a process that requires in-depth expertise, reducing developer productivity. To tackle these challenges, we introduce AutoSP: the first automated solution to automatically optimize LLM training for longer-contexts. AutoSP compiles models and applies a targeted set of optimizations: automated sequence parallelism, and long-context aware activation-checkpointing, to drastically enhance LLM trainability at negligible cost to throughput. Our evaluation demonstrates AutoSP's capability on both NVIDIA and AMD hardware, increasing training contexts by upto 2.7$\times$ and 2.5$\times$ respectively over competitive hand-written baseline at negligible cost to runtime performance.

中文摘要翻译: 大型语言模型在处理需要包含数万至数十万个词元的提示词的长上下文任务中展现了巨大效用。然而，现有的LLM训练库未能提供易于使用的高层抽象来优化长上下文训练，而是通过ZeRO-3/FSDP、张量并行和流水线并行等技术专注于对具有大量参数的模型进行优化。这迫使用户重写LLM训练库以将各种复杂的长上下文优化（如序列并行）组合到训练流程中；这个过程需要深入的专业知识，降低了开发者的生产力。为解决这些挑战，我们引入了AutoSP：首个自动优化LLM长上下文训练的自动化解决方案。AutoSP通过对模型进行编译，应用一组有针对性的优化——自动序列并行和长上下文感知的激活检查点——在吞吐量代价可忽略不计的情况下，显著增强LLM的可训练性。我们的评估展示了AutoSP在NVIDIA和AMD硬件上的能力，相比手工编写的最优基线，训练上下文长度分别提升高达2.7倍和2.5倍，且运行时性能开销可忽略不计。

### [81] [Anomaly Detection in Soil Heavy Metal Contamination Using Unsupervised Learning for Environmental Risk Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27102)
*Isaac Tettey Adjokatse,Samuel Senyo Koranteng,George Yamoah Afrifa,Theophilus Ansah-Narh,Marcellin Atemkeng,Joseph Bremang Tandoh,Kow Ahor Essel-Yorke,Richmond Opoku-Sarkodie,Rebecca Davis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究利用无监督机器学习（孤立森林、PCA重构误差、DBSCAN）检测加纳中部地区12个垃圾场土壤重金属异常污染模式，共识方法识别出6个稳健异常样本（7.7%），均集中于S3站点，异常样本的危害指数（HI）均值比正常样本高约70-80%，且PCA重构误差与HI呈强正相关（r≈0.8）。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 加纳快速城市化地区（尤其是非正规垃圾场）的土壤重金属污染对环境和公共健康构成持续威胁，传统聚合健康风险指数（如HI、ILCR）无法提供颗粒度的异常检测和空间定位，亟需客观、精细的异常识别方法以支持针对性场地优先排序和风险管理。

Method: 采用无监督机器学习框架：孤立森林（Isolation Forest）、PCA重构误差（PCA reconstruction error）和DBSCAN三种算法分别检测异常，并通过共识方法（consensus approach）筛选稳健异常；分析8种重金属（As, Cd, Cr, Cu, Hg, Ni, Pb, Zn）浓度及健康风险指数（HI、ILCR）。

Result: 孤立森林和PCA重构误差各识别12个异常样本（15.4%），DBSCAN未检出密度孤立点；共识方法锁定6个稳健异常（7.7%），全部集中于S3站点；异常样本HI均值比正常样本高约70-80%，且均超过HI=1阈值；PCA重构误差与HI呈强正相关（r≈0.8）；识别出三种异常类型：S3极端Cu富集、S4/S5异常低Ni、S9-S12中等多金属（Pb-Zn）共升。

Conclusion: 无监督机器学习能够提供超越聚合健康风险指数的颗粒度、客观洞察，实现对污染场地的针对性优先级排序和风险知情环境管理。

Original Abstract: Soil contamination by heavy metals poses a persistent environmental and public health concern in rapidly urbanising regions of Ghana, particularly at unregulated waste disposal sites. This study applies an unsupervised machine learning framework to detect and characterise anomalous heavy metal contamination patterns in soils from twelve waste sites and residential controls in the Central Region, of Ghana. Concentrations of eight metals (As, Cd, Cr, Cu, Hg, Ni, Pb, Zn) were analysed alongside standard health risk indices, including the Hazard Index (HI) and Incremental Lifetime Cancer Risk (ILCR). Isolation Forest and PCA reconstruction error each identified $12$ anomalous samples ($15.4\%$ of $78$ samples), while DBSCAN detected no density-isolated noise points. A consensus approach isolated six robust anomalies ($7.7\%)$, all spatially concentrated at a single site (S3). Anomalies exhibited approximately $70$--$80\%$ higher mean HI values than normal samples, with all consensus anomalies exceeding the HI$=1$ threshold. PCA reconstruction error showed a strong positive association with HI ($r \approx 0.8$), indicating consistency between multivariate deviation and health risk. Three distinct anomaly types were identified: extreme Cu enrichment at S3, anomalously low Ni at S4/S5, and moderate multi-metal (Pb--Zn) co-elevation at S9--S12. The results demonstrate that unsupervised machine learning provides granular, objective insight beyond aggregate indices, enabling targeted site prioritisation and risk-informed environmental management.

中文摘要翻译: 在加纳快速城市化的区域，重金属对土壤的污染构成了持续的环境与公共卫生问题，尤其出现在未受监管的废弃物处置场地。本研究采用无监督机器学习框架，检测并刻画了加纳中部地区12个垃圾场及居民对照区土壤中的异常重金属污染模式。分析了八种金属（As、Cd、Cr、Cu、Hg、Ni、Pb、Zn）的浓度，以及包括危害指数（HI）和增量终身癌症风险（ILCR）在内的标准健康风险指标。孤立森林和PCA重构误差各自识别出12个异常样本（占78个样本的15.4%），而DBSCAN未检测到密度孤立的噪声点。通过共识方法分离出6个稳健异常（7.7%），这些异常在空间上集中于单一站点（S3）。异常样本的HI均值比正常样本高出约70%-80%，所有共识异常均超过HI=1阈值。PCA重构误差与HI呈强正相关（r≈0.8），表明多变量偏差与健康风险之间具有一致性。识别出三种不同的异常类型：S3处的极端Cu富集、S4/S5处的异常低Ni，以及S9-S12处的中等多金属（Pb-Zn）共升。结果表明，无监督机器学习能够提供超越聚合指标的颗粒化、客观洞察，从而实现针对性的场地优先排序和风险知情的环境管理。

### [82] [Better Models, Faster Training: Sigmoid Attention for single-cell Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27124)
*Vijay Sadashivaiah,Georgios Dasoulas,Judith Mueller,Soumya Ghosh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出用sigmoid注意力机制替换softmax注意力机制来训练稳定的生物基础模型，发现sigmoid注意力在表征质量、训练速度和训练稳定性上均优于softmax，并开源了高效GPU核TritonSigmoid。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 训练稳定的生物基础模型需要重新思考注意力机制，因为softmax注意力存在固有的不稳定性问题。

Method: 使用sigmoid注意力作为softmax注意力的直接替代品，并设计了高效的GPU核TritonSigmoid。

Result: 在六个单细胞数据集上，sigmoid注意力实现了25%更高的细胞类型分离度、更好的细胞类型内聚性指标和更低的验证损失；训练速度比softmax快10%；在1.6亿参数的双向注意力模型压力测试中，softmax梯度爆炸四个数量级，而sigmoid保持稳定；TritonSigmoid在H100 GPU上达到515 TFLOPS，优于FlashAttention-2和FlashSigmoid。

Conclusion: Sigmoid注意力在生物基础模型上既具有理论基础又具有经验优越性。

Original Abstract: Training stable biological foundation models requires rethinking attention mechanisms: we find that using sigmoid attention as a drop in replacement for softmax attention a) produces better learned representations: on six diverse single-cell datasets, sigmoid achieves 25% higher cell-type separation, better cell-type cohesion metrics, and lower validation loss, b) faster training, models with sigmoid attention train up to 10% faster than their softmax counterparts, and c) more stable training by eliminating inherent sources of instability in softmax attention. We establish that sigmoid attention has globally bounded derivatives ($\leq 0.25$) as opposed to softmax, and a diagonal Jacobian structure in contrast with softmax's dense coupling, which together help alleviate training instabilities. In stress tests on 160M-parameter bidirectional attention models trained without gradient clipping on 8K-token sequences, softmax diverges catastrophically, with gradients exploding by four orders of magnitude, while sigmoid remains stable. Finally, we implement and open-source TritonSigmoid, an efficient GPU kernel that achieves 515 TFLOPS on H100 GPUs, outperforming both FlashAttention-2 and FlashSigmoid, with native padding support, which is essential for biological sequences. Our results establish sigmoid attention as both theoretically grounded and empirically superior for biological foundation models. Code is available at https://github.com/MSDLLCpapers/triton-sigmoid

中文摘要翻译: 训练稳定的生物基础模型需要重新思考注意力机制：我们发现使用sigmoid注意力作为softmax注意力的直接替代品，能够(a)产生更好的学习表征：在六个不同的单细胞数据集上，sigmoid实现了25%更高的细胞类型分离度、更好的细胞类型内聚性指标以及更低的验证损失；(b)更快的训练速度：采用sigmoid注意力的模型训练速度比softmax对应模型快10%；(c)更稳定的训练过程：消除了softmax注意力中固有的不稳定来源。我们证明了sigmoid注意力具有全局有界导数（≤0.25），而softmax则没有；并且具有对角雅可比矩阵结构，与softmax的密集耦合形成对比，这共同有助于缓解训练不稳定问题。在1.6亿参数的双向注意力模型压力测试中（不使用梯度裁剪，在8K令牌序列上训练），softmax出现灾难性发散，梯度爆炸达四个数量级，而sigmoid保持稳定。最后，我们实现并开源了TritonSigmoid，这是一个高效的GPU核，在H100 GPU上实现515 TFLOPS，性能优于FlashAttention-2和FlashSigmoid，并支持原生填充，这对于生物序列至关重要。我们的结果证明，sigmoid注意力在生物基础模型上既具有理论基础又具有经验优越性。代码已开源：https://github.com/MSDLLCpapers/triton-sigmoid

### [83] [How to Guide Your Flow: Few-Step Alignment via Flow Map Reward Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27147)
*Jerry Y. Huang,Justin Lin,Sheel Shah,Kartik Nair,Nicholas M. Boffi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出FMRG（流图奖励引导），将生成模型中的引导问题重新表述为确定性最优控制问题，利用流图实现无需训练、单轨迹的高效引导，在文本到图像任务中以极少的NFE达到或超越现有方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有引导方法要么需要昂贵的多粒子、多步方案，要么依赖理解不充分的近似，缺乏统一的理论框架。

Method: 将引导重新表述为确定性最优控制问题，推导出算法层次结构；基于流图在最优解中的自然出现，提出FMRG框架，利用流图同时进行积分和引导。

Result: 在文本到图像尺度上，FMRG在逆问题、风格迁移、人类偏好和VLM奖励等方面匹配或超越基线方法，仅需3次NFE，相比先前最先进方法实现至少一个数量级的加速。

Conclusion: 引导可被形式化为最优控制问题，流图是实现高效引导的关键工具；FMRG是一种无需训练、单轨迹的高效引导方法。

Original Abstract: In generative modeling, we often wish to produce samples that maximize a user-specified reward such as aesthetic quality or alignment with human preferences, a problem known as guidance. Despite their widespread use, existing guidance methods either require expensive multi-particle, many-step schemes or rely on poorly understood approximations. We reformulate guidance as a deterministic optimal control problem, yielding a hierarchy of algorithms that subsumes existing approaches at the coarsest level. We show that the flow map, an object of significant recent interest for its role in fast inference, arises naturally in the optimal solution. Based on this observation, we propose Flow Map Reward Guidance (FMRG): a training-free, single-trajectory framework that uses the flow map to both integrate and guide the flow. At text-to-image scale, FMRG matches or surpasses baselines across inverse problems, style transfer, human preferences, and VLM rewards with as few as 3 NFEs, giving at least an order-of-magnitude speedup in comparison to prior state of the art.

中文摘要翻译: 在生成建模中，我们通常希望产生能够最大化用户指定奖励（如审美质量或与人类偏好的一致性）的样本，这一问题被称为引导。尽管现有引导方法被广泛使用，但它们要么需要昂贵的多粒子、多步方案，要么依赖理解不充分的近似。我们将引导重新表述为一个确定性最优控制问题，从而推导出一个算法层次结构，该结构在最粗粒度上涵盖了现有方法。我们表明，流图——这一因在快速推理中的作用而在近期受到广泛关注的对象——在最优解中自然出现。基于这一观察，我们提出流图奖励引导（FMRG）：一种无需训练、单轨迹的框架，利用流图同时进行积分和引导。在文本到图像尺度上，FMRG在逆问题、风格迁移、人类偏好和VLM奖励等方面匹配或超越基线方法，仅需3次NFE，相比先前最先进方法实现了至少一个数量级的加速。

### [84] [Generalizing the Geometry of Model Merging Through Frechet Averages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27155)
*Marvin F. da Silva,Mohammed Adnan,Felix Dangel,Sageev Oore*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出将模型合并视为流形上的Fréchet平均，通过对称性不变的平均过程实现感知对称性的模型合并，并针对LoRA场景设计了实用算法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有模型合并方法在参数空间直接平均时，忽略了架构对称性导致的几何结构差异，且不仅几何结构需要对称性感知，平均过程本身也必须是对称性不变的。

Method: 将模型合并形式化为流形上的Fréchet平均——最小化测地距离之和；核心设计选择是度量、流形和距离近似；结合简化假设可包含Fisher合并；针对LoRA的商流形几何提出实用合并算法。

Result: 理论表明Fréchet平均在简化假设下包含Fisher合并作为特例；实验对比显示所提出的LoRA合并方法优于现有常用方法。

Conclusion: 要实现感知对称性的模型合并，必须同时保证几何结构和平均过程的对称性不变性；Fréchet平均为统一框架提供了通用解决方案；LoRA的商流形几何需要专门的合并算法。

Original Abstract: Model merging aims to combine multiple models into one without additional training. Naïve parameter-space averaging can be fragile under architectural symmetries, as their geometry does not take them into account. In this work we show that not only the geometry, but also the averaging procedure itself, must be symmetry-invariant to achieve symmetry-aware merges. Consequently, we propose a general solution: merging as Fréchet averaging, i.e., selecting parameters that minimize a sum of geodesic distances on an appropriate manifold. In this view, the key design choice is the overall geometry, i.e., the choice of metric, manifold, and distance approximation, that determines what it means for two models to be "close". We show that Fréchet averaging, combined with simplifying assumptions, contains Fisher merging. Building on this, we examine the particular case of low-rank adapters (LoRA), whose symmetries induce a distinct geometry: that of a quotient manifold. We outline the limitations of current LoRA merging methods, propose a practical algorithm for this setting, and show how they compare with other commonly used approaches.

中文摘要翻译: 模型合并旨在将多个模型组合成一个，无需额外训练。在参数空间中进行朴素平均可能因架构对称性而脆弱，因为其几何结构未考虑这些对称性。在这项工作中，我们表明，要实现感知对称性的合并，不仅几何结构，平均过程本身也必须是对称性不变的。因此，我们提出一个通用解决方案：将合并视为Fréchet平均，即在适当流形上选择最小化测地距离之和的参数。在此视角下，关键的设计选择是整体几何结构，即度量、流形和距离近似的选择，这决定了两个模型“接近”的含义。我们证明，结合简化假设的Fréchet平均包含了Fisher合并。基于此，我们考察了低秩适配器（LoRA）这一特例，其对称性引发了独特的几何结构——商流形。我们概述了当前LoRA合并方法的局限性，为此场景提出了一个实用算法，并展示了它们与其他常用方法的比较结果。

### [85] [Distributional Alignment Games for Answer-Level Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27166)
*Mehryar Mohri,Jon Schneider,Yifan Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一个博弈论框架（分布对齐博弈），将答案级别的语言模型微调问题转化为可解的投影问题，并通过纳什均衡证明其与原始优化问题的等价性，在数学推理任务上取得显著复杂度改进。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 答案级别微调（ALFT）旨在基于最终答案的正确性优化语言模型，而非依赖推理轨迹。然而直接优化该目标需要对海量潜在推理路径进行边缘化，计算上不可行。因此需要一种可计算的方法来解决这一困难。

Method: 提出一个博弈论框架——分布对齐博弈（Distributional Alignment Game），将ALFT建模为策略模型（生成器）与目标分布（辅助分布）之间的两玩家博弈。通过理论证明该博弈的纳什均衡等价于原始答案级优化问题的解，从而将不可解的边缘化问题转化为可解的投影问题，并据此设计了与GRPO兼容的高效算法（如Coherence-GRPO）。

Result: 该框架统一了多样性和自我改进（一致性）等近期方法，提出的Coherence-GRPO等算法在数学推理任务上实现了显著的复杂度增益。

Conclusion: 基于博弈论的变分视角为答案级微调提供了一种理论上严谨且计算可行的方法，能够统一多种现有方法并在复杂推理任务上提升效率。

Original Abstract: We focus on the problem of \emph{Answer-Level Fine-Tuning} (ALFT), where the goal is to optimize a language model based on the correctness or properties of its final answers, rather than the specific reasoning traces used to produce them. Directly optimizing answer-level objectives is computationally intractable due to the need to marginalize over the vast space of latent reasoning paths. To overcome this, we propose a general game-theoretical framework that lifts the problem to a \emph{Distributional Alignment Game}. We formulate ALFT as a two-player game between a Policy (the generator) and a Target (an auxiliary distribution). We prove that the Nash Equilibrium of this game corresponds exactly to the solution of the original answer-level optimization problem. This variational perspective transforms the intractable marginalization problem into a tractable projection problem. We demonstrate that this framework unifies recent approaches to diversity and self-improvement (coherence) and provide efficient algorithms compatible with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), such as Coherence-GRPO, yielding significant complexity gains in mathematical reasoning tasks.

中文摘要翻译: 我们关注答案级微调（Answer-Level Fine-Tuning, ALFT）问题，其目标是根据语言模型最终答案的正确性或属性来优化模型，而非依赖生成这些答案的具体推理轨迹。直接优化答案级目标在计算上不可行，因为需要对海量潜在推理路径进行边缘化。为克服这一困难，我们提出一个通用的博弈论框架，将问题提升为分布对齐博弈（Distributional Alignment Game）。我们将ALFT建模为一个两玩家博弈，参与方为策略模型（生成器）和目标分布（辅助分布）。我们证明该博弈的纳什均衡恰好对应于原始答案级优化问题的解。这一变分视角将不可解的边缘化问题转化为可解的投影问题。我们证明该框架能够统一近期关于多样性和自我改进（一致性）的方法，并提供与组相对策略优化（Group Relative Policy Optimization, GRPO）兼容的高效算法，例如Coherence-GRPO，从而在数学推理任务中取得显著的复杂度增益。

</details>


### [86] [Analytical Correction for Subsampling Bias in Drifting Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27239)
*Jiaru Zhang,Zeyun Deng,Juanwu Lu,Ziran Wang,Ruqi Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对漂移模型(drifting models)中minibatch质心估计的偏差问题，提出了分析性偏差校正(ABC)方法。该方法通过封闭形式的即插即用调整，将偏差从O(1/n)降至O(1/n^2)，且不引入一阶方差增加，在CIFAR-10上实现了更快的训练和更低的FID。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 漂移模型使用softmax加权质心进行一步生成，但实践中仅能获取每个分布的minibatch样本，导致经验估计的质心存在O(1/n)量级的点态偏差（由softmax自归一化引起）。直接修正该偏差需要全分布期望，计算不可行，因此需要一种可计算的偏差校正方法。

Method: 提出分析性偏差校正(ABC)方法：利用批内统计量近似偏差主导项，实现闭合形式的即插即用调整。理论上证明了ABC可将偏差从O(1/n)降至O(1/n^2)，且不引入一阶总方差增加，同时保持校正后质心的凸包包含性。实现上仅需额外两行代码，在编译执行下计算开销可忽略。

Result: 玩具实验验证了O(1/n)和O(1/n^2)的理论缩放关系。在CIFAR-10上，ABC降低了FID并加快了训练速度，在小n（偏差最显著）时收益最大。

Conclusion: ABC方法有效且高效地校正了漂移模型中minibatch质心的偏差，具有理论保证和实践优势。

Original Abstract: Drifting models are capable one-step generative models trained to follow a drifting field. The field combines attractive and repulsive softmax-weighted centroids over the data and current-generator distributions. In practice, only a minibatch of $n$ samples from each distribution is available, and each centroid is approximated by an empirical estimate. In this paper, we begin by showing that the minibatch centroid is in general a biased estimator of the target centroid, with a pointwise $O(1/n)$ bias arising from softmax self-normalization. Correcting this bias requires the expectation over the full distribution, which is intractable. We instead approximate the leading bias term from in-batch statistics and propose Analytical Bias Correction (ABC), a closed-form plug-in adjustment. We prove that ABC reduces the bias from $O(1/n)$ to $O(1/n^2)$, introduces no first-order increase in total variance, and preserves convex-hull containment of the corrected centroid. In practice, ABC requires only two additional lines of code and has negligible wall-time overhead under compiled execution. Toy experiments confirm the theoretical $O(1/n)$ and $O(1/n^2)$ scaling. On CIFAR-10, ABC reduces FID and trains faster, with the largest gains at small $n$, where the bias is most significant.

中文摘要翻译: 漂移模型是一种能够一步生成的可训练生成模型，其核心是跟随一个漂移场。该场结合了数据和当前生成器分布上的吸引性和排斥性softmax加权质心。在实践中，每个分布仅能获取n个样本的小批量，每个质心通过经验估计近似。本文首先证明，小批量质心通常是目标质心的有偏估计，其点态偏差为O(1/n)，由softmax自归一化引起。修正该偏差需要全分布的期望，这是不可计算的。我们转而利用批内统计量近似偏差主导项，提出了分析性偏差校正（ABC），一种闭合形式的即插即用调整。我们证明ABC将偏差从O(1/n)降至O(1/n^2)，不引入一阶总方差增加，并保持校正后质心的凸包包含性。在实践中，ABC仅需额外两行代码，在编译执行下运行时间开销可忽略。玩具实验验证了理论上的O(1/n)和O(1/n^2)缩放关系。在CIFAR-10上，ABC降低了FID并加快了训练速度，在小n（偏差最显著）时收益最大。

</details>


### [87] [Predicting Covariate-Driven Spatial Deformation for Nonstationary Gaussian Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27280)
*Minghao Gu,Weizhi Lin,Qiang Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对非平稳高斯过程的形变方法无法在协变量变化下进行预测的局限性，提出了一种将空间形变建模为协变量函数的预测性框架，通过李代数生成速度场刻画形变，并证明高阶交互项可截断，从而开发出高效的估计-推断算法，实现有限样本下的非平稳GP外推预测。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统的空间形变方法是一种静态方法，无法考虑协变量引起的空间相关性变化，因此在新的协变量条件下无法对非平稳高斯过程进行预测。本文旨在克服这一局限性，使形变方法具备预测能力。

Method: 本文将空间形变建模为协变量的函数，通过李代数中的速度场生成微分同胚形变，建立欧几里得协变量向量与形变空间之间的连接。理论证明在适度物理假设下可截断多协变量间的高阶交互作用，进而建立简洁的协变量驱动形变函数形式，并开发高效的估计-推断算法，用于有限协变量-形变样本对下的样本外非平稳GP预测。

Result: 仿真实验以及制造业和地统计学两个案例研究验证了该方法在样本外非平稳GP预测中的有效性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: 提出了一种基于协变量驱动形变的可预测非平稳高斯过程建模框架，理论上证明了高阶交互项的可截断性，算法上实现了高效估计与推断，实验上展现了良好的有效性和泛化性。

Original Abstract: Nonstationary Gaussian processes (GPs) are essential for modeling complex, locally heterogeneous spatial data. A common modeling approach is the spatial deformation method that warps the domain to recover isotropy. However, this static method does not account for changes in spatial correlation induced by covariates, limiting its ability to predict nonstationary GPs under new covariate conditions.
  To enable predictive modeling of the deformation method, we propose to model the spatial deformation as a function of covariates. The spaces of diffeomorphic deformations and Euclidean covariate vectors are connected by characterizing deformations as generated by velocity fields living in a Lie algebra. To overcome the estimation instability caused by high-order interactions between multiple covariates in a general Lie algebra, we prove that those interactions can be truncated with a moderate physical assumption. Based on the theoretical results, a concise functional form of deformations driven by multiple covariates can be established, and an efficient estimation-inference algorithm is developed for out-of-sample nonstationary GP prediction with limited covariate-deformation sample pairs. The effectiveness and generalizability of the method are demonstrated on a simulation study and two case studies, in the fields of manufacturing and geostatistics, respectively.

中文摘要翻译: 非平稳高斯过程对于建模复杂、局部异质的空间数据至关重要。一种常见的建模方法是空间形变法，通过对区域进行扭曲来恢复各向同性。然而，这种静态方法无法考虑由协变量引起的空间相关性变化，限制了其在新的协变量条件下对非平稳高斯过程进行预测的能力。为了赋予形变方法预测建模的能力，我们提出将空间形变建模为协变量的函数。通过将形变刻画为由李代数中的速度场生成，建立微分同胚形变空间与欧几里得协变量向量空间之间的连接。为克服多协变量在一般李代数中因高阶交互作用导致的估计不稳定性，我们证明在适度的物理假设下这些交互作用可以被截断。基于理论结果，可以建立由多协变量驱动的形变简洁函数形式，并开发出高效的估计-推断算法，用于在有限协变量-形变样本对下进行样本外非平稳高斯过程预测。通过仿真实验以及制造业和地统计学两个案例研究，验证了该方法的有效性和泛化能力。

### [88] [PINN-Cast: Exploring the Role of Continuous-Depth NODE in Transformers and Physics Informed Loss as Soft Physical Constraints in Short-term Weather Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27313)
*Hira Saleem,Flora Salim,Cormac Purcell*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种连续深度Transformer编码器用于天气预报，将神经常微分方程（Neural ODE）引入编码器块替代离散残差更新，并设计了双分支注意力模块和物理信息训练目标，在短时天气预报中优于离散Transformer基线模型和现有连续时间Neural ODE预测模型。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统数值天气预报计算成本高、工作流复杂；现有基于Transformer的数据驱动方法虽高效但忽略物理机制，且标准Transformer的离散层更新不适合建模平滑的潜空间动态。

Method: 1) 将编码器块中的离散残差更新替换为基于Neural ODE的连续更新，使用自适应数值积分求解；2) 设计双分支注意力模块，包含常规分块自注意力和对注意力logits施加导数算子的辅助分支；3) 提出物理信息训练目标，将物理一致性作为软约束加入损失函数。

Result: 在短时天气预报任务上，PINN-Cast优于标准离散Transformer基线和现有连续时间Neural ODE预测变体，验证了各模块的有效性和物理约束的重要性。

Conclusion: 连续深度Transformer编码器结合Neural ODE动态、双分支注意力和物理约束，能够有效提升数据驱动天气预报的精度和物理一致性。

Original Abstract: Operational weather prediction has long relied on physics-based numerical weather prediction (NWP), whose accuracy comes at the cost of substantial compute and complex simulation workflows. Recent transformer-based forecasters offer efficient data-driven alternatives, however transformers are physics-agnostic models. Additionally, standard transformer encoders evolve representations through discrete layer updates that may be less suited to modeling smooth latent dynamics. In this work, we propose a continuous-depth transformer encoder for weather forecasting that integrates Neural Ordinary Differential Equation (Neural ODE) dynamics within each encoder block. Specifically, we replace discrete residual updates with ODE-based updates solved using adaptive numerical integration. We also introduce a two-branch attention module that combines conventional patch-wise self-attention with an auxiliary branch that applies a derivative operator to attention logits, providing an additional change-sensitive interaction signal. To further align forecasts with governing principles, we propose a customized physics-informed training objective that enforces physical consistency as a soft constraint. We evaluate the proposed method against a standard discrete transformer baseline and an existing continuous-time Neural ODE forecasting variant, demonstrating the importance of PINN-Cast in short term weather forecasting.

中文摘要翻译: 业务天气预报长期以来依赖于基于物理的数值天气预报（NWP），其准确性以巨大的计算成本和复杂的模拟工作流为代价。近年来基于Transformer的预报器提供了高效的数据驱动替代方案，但Transformer是物理无关的模型。此外，标准Transformer编码器通过离散层更新来演化表征，这可能不太适合建模平滑的潜空间动态。本文提出了一种用于天气预报的连续深度Transformer编码器，将神经常微分方程（Neural ODE）动态引入每个编码器块中。具体而言，我们将离散残差更新替换为使用自适应数值积分求解的基于ODE的更新。我们引入了一个双分支注意力模块，将常规的分块自注意力与一个对注意力logits施加导数算子的辅助分支相结合，提供额外的变化敏感交互信号。为了进一步使预报与主导原理对齐，我们提出了一种定制化的物理信息训练目标，将物理一致性作为软约束施加。我们评估了所提方法相对于标准离散Transformer基线和现有连续时间Neural ODE预测变体的性能，证明了PINN-Cast在短时天气预报中的重要性。

### [89] [AG-TAL: Anatomically-Guided Topology-Aware Loss for Multiclass Segmentation of the Circle of Willis Using Large-Scale Multi-Center Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27357)
*Jialu Liu,Yue Cui,Shan Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种解剖引导的拓扑感知损失函数（AG-TAL），用于解决脑底动脉环（CoW）多类分割中的血管不连续和类间误分类问题。AG-TAL 结合了半径感知Dice损失、基于组卷积的断裂感知clDice损失和邻接感知共现损失，在多个数据集上显著提升了对小动脉的分割精度，并验证了其在阿尔茨海默病队列中的临床应用潜力。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有的深度学习方法对脑底动脉环（CoW）进行多类分割时，常出现血管不连续和不同类别间的误分类问题；同时，现有的拓扑损失函数在3D多类场景下计算成本过高，难以实际应用。

Method: 提出AG-TAL损失函数，包含三个组件：(1) 半径感知Dice损失，解决小血管的类别不平衡问题；(2) 基于组卷积的断裂感知clDice损失，高效保留局部连通性；(3) 邻接感知共现损失，利用解剖先验强制相邻动脉之间的清晰边界。

Result: AG-TAL在5折交叉验证中对所有CoW动脉的平均Dice得分为80.85%，小动脉提升1.05-3.09%；在6个独立数据集上，所有CoW动脉的Dice得分为74.46%-81.17%，小动脉提升2.20%-9.98%。

Conclusion: AG-TAL在多类CoW动脉识别中具有优越性，且能很好地泛化到多个独立数据集；在阿尔茨海默病队列中的信度分析和临床应用验证了其鲁棒性和发现影像学形态生物标志物的潜力。

Original Abstract: Accurate multiclass segmentation of the Circle of Willis (CoW) is essential for neurovascular disease management but remains challenging due to complex vascular topology and variable morphology. Existing deep learning methods often suffer from vascular discontinuities and inter-class misclassification, while current topological loss functions incur prohibitive computational costs in 3D multiclass settings. To address these limitations, we propose an Anatomically-Guided Topology-Aware Loss (AG-TAL) and introduce a large-scale, multi-center CoW dataset with unified annotations to facilitate robust model training. AG-TAL specifically integrates a radius-aware Dice loss to address class imbalance in small vessels, a breakage-aware clDice loss that utilizes group convolutions to efficiently preserve local connectivity, and an adjacency-aware co-occurrence loss that leverages anatomical priors to enforce distinct boundaries between neighboring arteries. Evaluated using 5-fold cross-validation, AG-TAL achieved an average Dice score of 80.85% for all CoW arteries, with small arteries notably higher by 1.05-3.09% compared to state-of-the-art methods. Across six independent datasets, the performance of AG-TAL achieved Dice scores ranging from 74.46% to 81.17% for all CoW arteries, with improvements of 2.20% to 9.98% for small arteries compared to other methods. This study demonstrates the superiority of AG-TAL in identifying multiclass CoW arteries and its ability to generalize well to multiple independent datasets. Furthermore, reliability analyses and clinical applications in an Alzheimer's disease cohort validate the AG-TAL's robustness and its potential for discovering imaging-based morphological biomarkers.

中文摘要翻译: 准确的脑底动脉环（Circle of Willis, CoW）多类分割对于神经血管疾病管理至关重要，但由于复杂的血管拓扑结构和形态变异，这一任务仍然具有挑战性。现有的深度学习方法常出现血管不连续和类间误分类问题，而当前的拓扑损失函数在3D多类场景下计算成本过高。为解决这些限制，我们提出了一种解剖引导的拓扑感知损失函数（Anatomically-Guided Topology-Aware Loss, AG-TAL），并引入了一个大规模、多中心的CoW数据集及其统一标注，以促进鲁棒的模型训练。AG-TAL具体集成了：(1) 半径感知Dice损失，以解决小血管中的类别不平衡问题；(2) 基于组卷积的断裂感知clDice损失，高效保留局部连通性；(3) 邻接感知共现损失，利用解剖先验强制相邻动脉之间的清晰边界。通过5折交叉验证评估，AG-TAL对所有CoW动脉的平均Dice得分为80.85%，其中小动脉相比现有最优方法提升了1.05%-3.09%。在六个独立数据集上，AG-TAL对所有CoW动脉的Dice得分范围为74.46%-81.17%，小动脉相比其他方法提升了2.20%-9.98%。本研究证明了AG-TAL在多类CoW动脉识别中的优越性及其对多个独立数据集的良好泛化能力。此外，在阿尔茨海默病队列中的信度分析和临床应用验证了AG-TAL的鲁棒性及其发现基于影像学形态生物标志物的潜力。

### [90] [Stable but Wrong: An Inference Limit in Galactic Archaeology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27368)
*Zhipeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了一个关键发现：在银河考古学中，当观测数据质量（信噪比和视差精度）处于特定区间时，即使统计不确定性很小，从恒星光谱推断的年龄-金属丰度关系（AMR）及其衍生形成时标也会产生0.5-1 Gyr的系统性偏差，导致一个“稳定但错误”的推断状态。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 质疑观测科学中的核心假设——即随着样本量增大和不确定性减小，推断结果应收敛到真实物理量。具体在银河考古学领域，检验观测质量是否会对恒星年龄推断引入系统性偏差，从而影响对银盘形成历史的解读。

Method: 使用大量次巨星样本，分析观测质量参数空间（信噪比和视差精度）对年龄推断的影响，并以独立的地震学参考为标准进行比较。

Result: 在观测质量的特定参数区间内，推断的形成时标相对于独立的地震学参考存在0.5-1 Gyr的系统性偏移，而统计不确定性仍然很小，形成了“稳定但错误”的推断状态。

Conclusion: 观测质量可能导致系统性偏差，使得大样本下看似可靠的推断结果实际上偏离真实物理量，这对依赖大数据的观测科学提出了重要警示。

Original Abstract: Statistical inference in observational science typically relies on a fundamental assumption: as sample size increases and uncertainties decrease, the inferred results should converge to the true physical quantities. This assumption underpins the notion that big data lead to more reliable conclusions. In Galactic archaeology, stellar ages inferred from spectroscopic surveys are widely used to reconstruct the formation history of the Milky Way disk. The age metallicity relation (AMR) and its derived formation timescale are often regarded as key physical diagnostics of early disk evolution. This interpretation carries an implicit premise: that observational quality does not introduce systematic bias into age inference. Here we show that this premise may fail. Using a large sample of subgiant stars, we identify a region in the observational quality parameter space (signal-to-noise ratio and parallax precision) where the inferred formation timescale exhibits a systematic offset of 0.5-1 Gyr relative to an independent asteroseismic reference, while the statistical uncertainties remain small, thus producing a stable-but-wrong inference state.

中文摘要翻译: 观测科学中的统计推断通常依赖一个基本假设：随着样本量增加和不确定性减小，推断结果应收敛到真实物理量。这一假设支撑着"大数据带来更可靠结论"的观点。在银河考古学中，从光谱巡天推断出的恒星年龄被广泛用于重建银盘的 formation 历史。年龄-金属丰度关系（AMR）及其衍生形成时标通常被视为早期银盘演化的关键物理诊断。这种解释隐含了一个前提：观测质量不会对年龄推断引入系统性偏差。在本文中，我们证明这一前提可能不成立。通过使用大量次巨星样本，我们在观测质量参数空间（信噪比和视差精度）中发现了一个区域，在该区域内推断的形成时标相对于独立的地震学参考存在0.5-1 Gyr的系统性偏移，而统计不确定性仍然很小，从而产生了一种稳定但错误的推断状态。

### [91] [Detecting is Easy, Adapting is Hard: Local Expert Growth for Visual Model-Based Reinforcement Learning under Distribution Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27411)
*Haiyang Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出JEPA-Indexed Local Expert Growth方法，通过冻结JEPA表示进行问题索引，为每个聚类训练局部残差专家来修正动作，在不损害分布内性能的前提下显著提升视觉MBRL在分布偏移下的表现。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 视觉MBRL智能体在训练分布上表现良好，但测试环境发生分布偏移时性能急剧下降。现有响应方法（如规划惩罚、直接微调、全局残差校正、粗粒度门控）要么无法改善闭环控制，要么损害分布内性能。因此需要一种既能应对分布偏移又不损害原始性能的方法。

Method: 提出JEPA-Indexed Local Expert Growth方法：使用冻结的JEPA表示仅用于问题索引，将偏移场景聚类；为每个聚类训练独立的残差专家，在原始控制器基础上添加局部动作修正；原始控制器本身不做修改。同时提出harder-pair变体以提高稳定性。

Result: 通过paired-bootstrap评估发现：原始naive-preference变体在严格测试下不稳定，而harder-pair变体在所有四种偏移条件下均产生统计显著的OOD改进，同时保持ID性能不变。学习的专家在再次遇到相同偏移时仍有效。自动ID拒绝可通过简单密度模型实现，但OOD子类间的细粒度判别受限于表示能力。

Conclusion: 视觉MBRL在分布偏移下的主要挑战不在于检测环境变化，而在于识别变化后施加正确的局部动作修正。JEPA-Indexed Local Expert Growth方法通过增量知识积累的方式实现适应，避免了重复的全模型重训。

Original Abstract: Visual model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) agents can perform well on the training distribution, but often break down once the test environment shifts. In visual MBRL, recognizing that a shift has occurred is often the easier part; the harder part is turning that recognition into useful action-level correction. We study several ways of responding to shift, including planning penalties, direct fine-tuning, global residual correction, and coarse gating. In our experiments, these approaches either do not improve closed-loop control or hurt in-distribution (ID) performance. Based on these negative results, we propose JEPA-Indexed Local Expert Growth. The method uses a frozen JEPA representation only for problem indexing, while cluster-specific residual experts add local action corrections on top of the original controller. The baseline controller itself is not modified. Using paired-bootstrap evaluation, we find that the original naive-preference variant is not stable under stricter testing. In contrast, the harder-pair variant produces statistically significant OOD improvements on all four evaluated shift conditions while preserving ID performance. The learned experts also remain useful when the same shift is encountered again, which supports the view of adaptation as incremental knowledge growth rather than repeated full retraining. We further show that automatic ID rejection can be achieved with simple density models, whereas fine-grained discrimination among OOD sub-families is limited by the representation. Overall, the results indicate that, for visual MBRL under distribution shift, the main challenge is not simply noticing that the environment has changed, but applying the right local action correction after the change has been recognized.

中文摘要翻译: 基于视觉的模型强化学习（MBRL）智能体在训练分布上表现良好，但一旦测试环境发生偏移，其性能往往会崩溃。在视觉MBRL中，识别到偏移发生通常较为容易；更难的是将这种识别转化为有效的动作级修正。我们研究了多种应对偏移的方式，包括规划惩罚、直接微调、全局残差校正以及粗粒度门控。在我们的实验中，这些方法要么无法改善闭环控制，要么损害了分布内（ID）性能。基于这些负面结果，我们提出了JEPA索引局部专家增长方法。该方法仅使用冻结的JEPA表示进行问题索引，同时为每个聚类专门的残差专家，在原始控制器之上添加局部动作修正。基线控制器本身不做修改。通过配对自举评估，我们发现原始朴素偏好变体在更严格的测试下不稳定。相比之下，困难配对变体在所有四种评估的偏移条件下均产生了统计显著的分布外（OOD）改进，同时保持了分布内性能。所学到的专家在再次遭遇相同偏移时仍然有效，这支持了将适应视为增量知识积累而非重复全模型重训的观点。我们进一步表明，使用简单的密度模型即可实现自动分布内拒绝，而OOD子类之间的细粒度判别则受限于表示能力。总体而言，结果表明，对于分布偏移下的视觉MBRL，主要挑战不在于简单地注意到环境发生了变化，而在于识别到变化后施加正确的局部动作修正。

</details>


### [92] [ChipLingo: A Systematic Training Framework for Large Language Models in EDA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27415)
*Lei Li,Xingwen Yu,Jianguo Ni,Junxuan Zhu,Jieqiong Zhang,Jian Zhao,Zhi Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出ChipLingo，一个面向EDA领域的LLM系统化训练流程，包含领域语料构建、领域自适应预训练和指令对齐三个阶段，并构建了EDA-Bench基准。实验表明ChipLingo-8B和32B在EDA任务上显著优于同规模基座模型，部分接近闭源商用模型，验证了系统化领域训练对知识密集型EDA任务的价值。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: LLM在EDA这一知识密集且文档驱动的工程领域直接应用面临三大挑战：领域专业知识不足、跨工具知识混淆、领域训练后检索增强生成（RAG）性能下降。现有通用大模型难以直接胜任EDA场景，亟需系统化的领域适应方案。

Method: ChipLingo包含三个阶段：(1) 领域语料构建：多源数据整理与QA增强；(2) 领域自适应预训练：对比不同参数训练策略（如LoRA与Partial FT）；(3) 指令对齐与RAG场景训练：在多种检索条件下进行训练。同时构建了EDA-Bench内部基准。

Result: ChipLingo-8B在EDA-Bench上达到59.7%准确率，超越同规模基座模型及部分更大规模通用模型；ChipLingo-32B达到70.02%，接近领先的闭源商用模型。进一步分析表明：QA增强提升领域性能，Partial FT比LoRA在领域适应与通用能力保持之间取得更好平衡，显式RAG场景训练缓解了领域训练后检索利用率下降的问题。

Conclusion: 系统化的领域训练对于知识密集型EDA任务具有重要实用价值，ChipLingo为未来EDA智能体和外部知识驱动系统提供了基础支持。

Original Abstract: With the rapid advancement of semiconductor technology, Electronic Design Automation (EDA) has become an increasingly knowledge-intensive and document-driven engineering domain. To address these issues, this paper presents ChipLingo, a systematic training pipeline for domain-adapted LLMs tailored to EDA scenarios.

We also curate an internal benchmark, EDA-Bench, covering representative EDA tool scenarios, with plans for public release.

ChipLingo-32B reaches 70.02%, approaching leading closed-source commercial models. Further analysis shows that QA augmentation improves domain performance, Partial FT offers a better balance between adaptation and general capability retention than LoRA, and explicit RAG scenario training mitigates the decline in retrieval utilization after domain training. These results demonstrate the practical value of systematic domain training for knowledge-intensive EDA tasks and provide a foundation for future EDA agents and external-knowledge-driven systems.

中文摘要翻译: 随着半导体技术的快速发展，电子设计自动化（EDA）已成为一个日益知识密集和文档驱动的工程领域。尽管大语言模型（LLM）已展现出强大的通用能力，但由于领域专业知识有限、跨工具知识混淆以及领域训练后检索增强生成（RAG）性能下降，将其直接应用于EDA仍面临挑战。为解决这些问题，本文提出了ChipLingo，一个面向EDA场景的系统化领域自适应LLM训练流程。ChipLingo包含三个阶段：多源数据整理与QA增强的领域语料构建、不同参数训练策略对比的领域自适应预训练，以及多种检索条件下结合RAG场景训练的指令对齐。我们还构建了一个内部基准EDA-Bench，涵盖代表性EDA工具场景，并计划公开发布。实验表明，ChipLingo-8B在EDA-Bench上达到59.7%的准确率，超越了同规模基座模型和部分更大规模的通用模型。ChipLingo-32B达到70.02%，接近领先的闭源商用模型。进一步分析表明，QA增强提升了领域性能，Partial FT在领域适应与通用能力保持之间比LoRA实现了更好的平衡，显式RAG场景训练缓解了领域训练后检索利用率下降的问题。这些结果证明了系统化领域训练对知识密集型EDA任务的实用价值，并为未来的EDA智能体和外部知识驱动系统奠定了基础。

### [93] [AdaBFL: Multi-Layer Defensive Adaptive Aggregation for Bzantine-Robust Federated Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27434)
*Zehui Tang,Yuchen Liu,Feihu Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出AdaBFL，一种基于三层防御机制的自适应聚合方法，用于在非凸和非独立同分布设置下抵御拜占庭攻击，实验表明其优于现有算法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 联邦学习容易受到投毒攻击（拜占庭攻击），现有的鲁棒方法难以平衡地对多种攻击进行防御，或依赖服务器拥有数据集，存在局限性。

Method: 提出一种多层防御自适应聚合方法AdaBFL，基于新颖的三层防御机制，能够自适应调整防御算法的权重以应对复杂的攻击，并在非凸非独立同分布数据上提供了收敛性证明。

Result: 在多个数据集上的综合实验表明，AdaBFL在防御性能上优于可比的对比算法。

Original Abstract: Federated learning (FL) is a popular distributed learning paradigm in machine learning, which enables multiple clients to collaboratively train models under the guidance of a server without exposing private client data. However, FL's decentralized nature makes it vulnerable to poisoning attacks, where malicious clients can submit corrupted models to manipulate the system. To counter such attacks, although various Byzantine-robust methods have been proposed, these methods struggle to provide balanced defense against multiple types of attacks or rely on possessing the dataset in the server. To deal with these drawbacks, thus, we propose an effective multi-layer defensive adaptive aggregation for Bzantine-robust federated learning (AdaBFL) based on a novel three-layer defensive mechanism, which can adaptively adjust the weights of defense algorithms to counter complex attacks. Moreover, we provide convergence properties of our AdaBFL method under the non-convex setting on non-iid data. Comprehensive experiments across multiple datasets validate the superiority of our AdaBFL over the comparable algorithms.

中文摘要翻译: 联邦学习（FL）是机器学习中一种流行的分布式学习范式，它使多个客户端能够在服务器的指导下协同训练模型，而无需暴露客户端的私有数据。然而，FL的去中心化特性使其容易受到投毒攻击，恶意客户端可能提交被篡改的模型来操纵系统。为了应对此类攻击，尽管已有多种拜占庭鲁棒方法被提出，但这些方法难以平衡地对多种类型的攻击进行防御，或者依赖于服务器拥有数据集。为解决这些缺陷，我们提出了一种有效的基于多层防御的自适应聚合方法AdaBFL，用于拜占庭鲁棒联邦学习。该方法基于一种新颖的三层防御机制，能够自适应调整防御算法的权重以应对复杂的攻击。此外，我们提供了AdaBFL方法在非独立同分布数据上的非凸设置下的收敛性性质。多个数据集上的综合实验验证了AdaBFL相较于可比算法的优越性。

### [94] [ABC: Any-Subset Autoregression via Non-Markovian Diffusion Bridges in Continuous Time and Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27443)
*Gabe Guo,Thanawat Sornwanee,Lutong Hao,Elon Litman,Stefano Ermon,Jose Blanchet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出ABC（任意子集自回归模型），通过非马尔可夫扩散桥在连续时空中建模随机过程，解决现有扩散模型在条件生成中的三个关键局限。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有扩散模型在生成连续时间连续空间随机过程（如视频、天气预报）时存在三个关键局限：(1)噪声到数据的演化无法捕捉物理时间相近状态间的结构相似性，低步数下积分不稳定；(2)注入的随机噪声对物理过程的时间间隔不敏感，导致动力学不准确；(3)忽略了对任意子集状态（如不规则采样时间步、未来观测）的条件约束。

Method: 提出ABC（Any-Subset Autoregressive Models via Non-Markovian Diffusion Bridges），核心是使用一个连续的随机微分方程（SDE），其时间变量和中间状态跟踪真实时间和过程状态。通过路径空间上的测度变换推导SDE动力学，支持对状态历史和未来的任意子集进行路径依赖的条件约束。学习时使用路径和时间依赖的去噪分数匹配扩展。

Result: 在视频生成和天气预报等多个领域，ABC方法在性能上优于现有竞争方法。

Conclusion: ABC通过让SDE的时间变量和中间状态与真实物理过程对齐，同时支持任意子集条件约束，有效克服了现有扩散模型的局限性，在多个下游任务中展现出优越性能。

Original Abstract: Generating continuous-time, continuous-space stochastic processes (e.g., videos, weather forecasts) conditioned on partial observations (e.g., first and last frames) is a fundamental challenge. Existing approaches, (e.g., diffusion models), suffer from key limitations: (1) noise-to-data evolution fails to capture structural similarity between states close in physical time and has unstable integration in low-step regimes; (2) random noise injected is insensitive to the physical process's time elapsed, resulting in incorrect dynamics; (3) they overlook conditioning on arbitrary subsets of states (e.g., irregularly sampled timesteps, future observations). We propose ABC: Any-Subset Autoregressive Models via Non-Markovian Diffusion Bridges in Continuous Time and Space. Crucially, we model the process with one continual SDE whose time variable and intermediate states track the real time and process states. This has provable advantages: (1) the starting point for generating future states is the already-close previous state, rather than uninformative noise; (2) random noise injection scales with physical time elapsed, encouraging physically plausible dynamics with similar time-adjacent states. We derive SDE dynamics via changes-of-measure on path space, yielding another advantage: (3) path-dependent conditioning on arbitrary subsets of the state history and/or future. To learn these dynamics, we derive a path- and time-dependent extension of denoising score matching. Our experiments show ABC's superiority to competing methods on multiple domains, including video generation and weather forecasting.

中文摘要翻译: 生成基于部分观测（如首尾帧）条件下连续时间、连续空间的随机过程（例如视频、天气预报）是一项基本挑战。现有方法（如扩散模型）存在关键局限：(1)噪声到数据的演化无法捕捉物理时间相近状态间的结构相似性，且在低步数模式下积分不稳定；(2)注入的随机噪声对物理过程的时间间隔不敏感，导致动力学不正确；(3)忽略了对任意子集状态（如不规则采样的时间步、未来观测）的条件约束。我们提出ABC：基于连续时空中非马尔可夫扩散桥的任意子集自回归模型。关键在于，我们使用一个连续的随机微分方程（SDE）来建模该过程，其时间变量和中间状态跟踪真实时间和过程状态。这具有可证明的优势：(1)生成未来状态的起点是已经接近的上一个状态，而非无信息的噪声；(2)随机噪声注入与物理时间间隔成比例，鼓励生成物理上合理且时间相邻状态相似的动力学。我们通过路径空间上的测度变换推导SDE动力学，从而获得另一个优势：(3)对状态历史和/或未来的任意子集进行路径依赖的条件约束。为学习这些动力学，我们推导了路径和时间依赖的去噪分数匹配扩展。实验表明，ABC在视频生成和天气预报等多个领域优于竞争方法。

</details>


### [95] [Improving Graph Few-shot Learning with Hyperbolic Space and Denoising Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27462)
*Yonghao Liu,Jialu Sun,Wei Pang,Fausto Giunchiglia,Ximing Li,Xiaoyue Feng,Renchu Guan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出IMPRESS框架，通过双曲空间表示学习和去噪扩散机制，解决了图小样本学习中欧氏空间无法捕捉层级结构以及支持样本分布偏移的问题，在理论上实现了更紧的泛化界，在多个基准数据集上持续优于现有方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有图小样本学习方法存在两个关键缺陷：(1) 元训练阶段在欧氏空间中进行节点表示学习，无法捕捉真实图数据中固有的层级结构；(2) 元测试阶段拟合仅由少量支持样本得到的经验目标分布，当该分布与真实分布存在显著偏差时性能下降。

Method: 提出IMPRESS框架，核心包括：(1) 在双曲空间中学习节点表示，以更好地捕捉图数据的层级结构；(2) 通过去噪扩散机制丰富支持分布，缓解小样本下的分布偏移问题。

Result: 理论上，IMPRESS实现了更紧的泛化界；实验上，在多个基准数据集上一致优于竞争基线方法。

Conclusion: IMPRESS通过双曲空间表示与去噪扩散机制有效解决了图小样本学习的两个关键局限，理论分析与实验结果均验证了其有效性。

Original Abstract: Graph few-shot learning, which focuses on effectively learning from only a small number of labeled nodes to quickly adapt to new tasks, has garnered significant research attention. Despite recent advances in graph few-shot learning that have demonstrated promising performance, existing methods still suffer from several key limitations. First, during the meta-training phase, these methods typically perform node representation learning in Euclidean space, which often fails to capture the inherently hierarchical structure existing in real-world graph data. Second, during the meta-testing phase, they usually fit an empirical target distribution derived from only a few support samples, even when this distribution significantly deviates from the true underlying distribution. To address these issues, we propose IMPRESS, a novel framework that IMproves graPh few-shot learning with hypeRbolic spacE and denoiSing diffuSion. Specifically, our model learns node representations in a hyperbolic space and enriches the support distribution through denoising diffusion mechanisms. Theoretically, IMPRESS achieves a tighter generalization bound. Empirically, IMPRESS consistently outperforms competitive baselines across multiple benchmark datasets.

中文摘要翻译: 图小样本学习专注于如何从仅有的少量标记节点中高效学习以快速适应新任务，该方向已引起广泛研究关注。尽管近期图小样本学习方法展现出令人鼓舞的性能，现有方法仍存在若干关键局限。首先，在元训练阶段，这些方法通常在欧氏空间中进行节点表示学习，这往往无法捕捉真实图数据中固有的层级结构。其次，在元测试阶段，它们通常拟合仅由少量支持样本得到的经验目标分布，即使该分布与真实分布存在显著偏离。为解决这些问题，我们提出IMPRESS——一个通过双曲空间与去噪扩散改进图小样本学习的新框架。具体而言，我们的模型在双曲空间中学习节点表示，并通过去噪扩散机制丰富支持分布。理论上，IMPRESS实现了更紧的泛化界。实验上，IMPRESS在多个基准数据集上一致优于竞争基线方法。

### [96] [FMCL: Class-Aware Client Clustering with Foundation Model Representations for Heterogeneous Federated Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27510)
*Mahad Ali,Laura J. Brattain*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出FMCL框架，利用冻结的基础模型为每个客户端生成类级嵌入原型，通过一次聚类实现联邦学习中的客户端分组，无需额外通信且与下游模型架构无关，有效提升了异构数据下的联邦学习性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有聚类联邦学习方法依赖原始数据统计量、模型参数或启发式相似度度量，难以捕捉跨异构域数据的类别级语义结构，且通常需要迭代协调，通信开销大。

Method: 使用冻结的基础模型为每个客户端计算类级嵌入原型，通过类感知表示之间的余弦距离衡量客户端相似性，在训练前进行一次聚类，后续联邦优化过程中无需额外通信，且与下游模型架构无关。

Result: 在异构基准测试上的大量实验表明，FMCL在非独立同分布数据划分下相比现有聚类方法提升了联邦学习性能，并实现了更稳定的聚类行为。

Conclusion: FMCL通过一次性的类感知客户端聚类，有效解决了统计异质性下的联邦学习性能退化问题，是一种高效、鲁棒且与模型架构无关的聚类联邦学习方案。

Original Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) enables collaborative model training across distributed clients without sharing raw data, yet its performance deteriorates under statistical heterogeneity. Clustered Federated Learning addresses this challenge by grouping similar clients and training separate models per cluster. However, existing clustering strategies often rely on raw data statistics, model parameters, or heuristic similarity measures that fail to capture class-level semantic structure across heterogeneous domains and frequently require iterative coordination. We propose FMCL, a one-shot, class-aware client clustering framework that leverages foundation model representations to construct semantic client signatures. Using a frozen foundation model, FMCL computes class-level embedding prototypes for each client and measures similarity via cosine distance between their class-aware representations. Clustering is performed once prior to training, introducing no additional communication during federated optimization and remaining agnostic to the downstream model architecture. Extensive experiments across heterogeneous benchmarks demonstrate that FMCL improves federated performance and yields more stable clustering behavior compared to existing clustering-based methods under non-identically distributed data partitioning.

中文摘要翻译: 联邦学习（FL）能够在分布式客户端之间实现协作模型训练而无需共享原始数据，但其性能在统计异质性下会退化。聚类联邦学习通过将相似客户端分组并为每个聚类训练独立模型来应对这一挑战。然而，现有的聚类策略通常依赖于原始数据统计量、模型参数或启发式相似度度量，这些方法难以捕捉跨异构域的类别级语义结构，并且常常需要迭代协调。我们提出FMCL，一种一次性、类感知的客户端聚类框架，利用基础模型表示来构建语义客户端签名。FMCL使用冻结的基础模型为每个客户端计算类级嵌入原型，并通过其类感知表示之间的余弦距离来度量相似性。聚类在训练前一次性完成，在联邦优化过程中不引入额外通信，并且与下游模型架构无关。在异构基准测试上的大量实验表明，在非独立同分布数据划分下，FMCL相比现有基于聚类的方法提升了联邦学习性能，并实现了更稳定的聚类行为。
